Tension Between U.S. and Japan

U.S. Secretary of War's Annual Report Opposes Philippine Independence and Advocates for Expanding the Army and Air Force

Washington, 2nd (National News Agency) – In his annual report submitted to the President, U.S. Army Chief of Staff Harbord stated that the Hawes-Cutting Philippine Independence Act does not provide solutions to the significant problems that will arise after independence. The bill prematurely requires the United States to stipulate future tax regulations for Philippine goods that will no longer be exempt from import duties into the United States, without considering the far-reaching social and economic consequences once independence is achieved. The report also includes recommendations from Chief of Staff MacArthur to expand the army by 40 percent and from Assistant Secretary of War Davison to continue the construction of aircraft.

Washington, 2nd (Reuters) – In his annual report to the President, the Secretary of War requested that the U.S. standing army be increased to 14,000 officers and 164,000 soldiers, with generous pay and all new-style weaponry. The Secretary of War opposes granting the Philippines independence within twenty years because the political situation in the East is currently unsettled. It is noted that the current U.S. standing army consists of 12,000 officers and 121,000 soldiers.

Washington, 3rd (National News Agency) – Today, Mr. Banker, advisor to the Chinese government, stated that he will begin to lobby senators to oppose the Hawes-Cutting Philippine Independence Act because the tax provisions in the bill will greatly harm the businesses controlled by Chinese residing in the Philippines. The bill stipulates that tariffs on Philippine goods will gradually increase from the passage of the bill until the establishment of the Philippine constitution. Banker stated that he will continue to oppose the bill until he receives assurance that it will be amended to protect Chinese businesses and prevent the exclusion of Chinese after Philippine independence. He claims to have considerable support for his position.

White House Continues Discussion of War Debt Issues

Stimson Indicates No Need to Respond to British and French Notes

U.S. May Temporarily Accommodate Debtors by Allowing Revised Interest Payments

Washington, 2nd (National News Agency) – Today, President Hoover, Secretary of State Stimson, and Treasury Secretary Mills held their second meeting to discuss the war debt issue, lasting a considerable time. After the meeting, when Secretary Stimson returned to the State Department, reporters asked when the U.S. reply would be drafted. Stimson replied that there may be no need to reply. He also said that the discussion had not yet yielded any results. According to international custom, notes from friendly nations must be answered. Stimson's statement that there may be no need to reply to the British and French notes, without further explanation, has led to various speculations and rumors. Some say that the State Department may soon receive unofficial documents from the British and French embassies, while others say that the President is discussing potential solutions with the Secretary of State and the Treasury Secretary, and has decided to continue discussions for at least another day. According to sources close to the government, tomorrow is Saturday, and the commodity and stock markets will only be open for half a day. Although the U.S. government's attitude cannot be decided immediately, it should not cause a major impact. However, the price declines in all markets today were purely due to the uncertainty of the war debt issue, indicating its seriousness.

President Hoover Hesitates

Washington, 2nd (National News Agency) – According to reliable sources, the President appears to be still hesitating on the war debt issue. It is rumored that he will submit a special report to Congress next week because the President considers this matter extremely important and will not address it in the regular report along with other economic issues. He will prepare a special report detailing the government's position. The original proposal to have a separate committee handle the war debt issue is said to have lost its momentum. Official circles have acknowledged that Treasury Secretary Mills may be able to announce, before December 15th, a temporary accommodation regarding the ninety-day notice clause in the war debt agreement, allowing Britain, France, and other debtor nations to defer principal payments, but interest payments must still be paid as scheduled.

Borah Believes British Note is Justified

Washington, 2nd (Havas) – Senator Borah, Chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, believes that outright cancellation or reduction of war debts is not enough to improve the world's economic situation. He also said, "Regarding the world's economic situation, my opinion is completely the same as the British note. The British note states that as long as various reasons for reducing confidence exist, the countries of the world will not be able to revive commerce. Not only will they not be able to revive commerce, but they will also not be able to find a way to restore the structure of commerce to normal. I deeply agree with this view. However, although the war debt issue is closely related to reducing confidence, it is not the only reason. The British note describes the terrifying state of global decline in great detail. To attempt to save it, no palliative measures or ineffective plans can succeed," and so on.

Tear Gas is No Match for Bottles and Rocks

American Hungry People Clash with Police

Wilmington (Delaware), 2nd (National News Agency) – Tonight, the petitioning team of hungry people had its first clash with the police here. The hungry people were holding a meeting when the police ordered them to disperse. When the hungry people refused, the police attempted to use force. Suddenly, bottles and stones were thrown from the crowd. The police then called for reinforcements and attacked with tear gas, immediately dispersing the hungry people. There were about 1,200 of them, intending to enter Washington on Monday morning together after the western hungry people's petitioning team arrived. Now that a clash has occurred, their leaders fear that it will be difficult to organize the team to enter the capital. They will have to sneak into the capital individually and then gather. Most of them are still able to maintain order, but since a few unruly elements have caused disturbances, a clash was unavoidable.

Congress Remains Firm

Washington, 2nd (Havas) – People close to the government say that President Hoover seems to have acknowledged the reasons presented in the British reply are very persuasive. However, many senators have stated that they will not change their stance. They have adopted a hostile attitude towards him, no different from their animosity towards Britain. Political figures here believe that the European debtor nations are insisting on delaying debt payments because President Hoover has secretly encouraged them. Hoover may even have corresponded with the debtor nations and made allowances without the knowledge of the U.S. Congress, which is also an unfounded accusation.

Washington, 2nd (Republican News Agency) – Speaker of the House Garner stated that although he knows that Congress will not approve the deferral of war debts, in his judgment, it is more beneficial in all respects for the United States to insist on payment. Garner's remarks are generally considered to represent the majority opinion in Congress, indicating that the attitude of members of both houses towards war debts remains unchanged. However, judging from Borah's words, there are also some in Congress who advocate for compromise, but their number is small.

Retaliation by Britain is of No Benefit

Warning from U.S. Senator

Washington, 2nd (Reuters) – Today, the U.S. Congress issued stern statements regarding the deferral of war debts. Senator Smoot said that if Britain imposes trade restrictions on the United States after paying its debts, then in his opinion, the victim would not be the United States, but Britain itself. Senator Harrison said that Britain's exaggerated talk of the possibility of disaster, its implied threats of actively managing exchange rates or increasing retaliatory plans, cannot change the United States' calm determination to oppose war debt cancellation or deferral.

Defaulting on Debt is Dishonorable

Roosevelt's Statement

Washington, 2nd (Reuters) – After Secretary of State Stimson and Treasury Secretary Mills conferred for several hours at the White House, a person said that we have not yet decided on the second step. It is expected that President Hoover's statement to Congress will be a reply to Britain and France. American newspapers are paying close attention to the British note, but they know that if Congress does not change its attitude, then there is ultimately nothing that can be done. The Christian Science Monitor said, "We will ultimately sell the world a sad image." The New York Times' Washington dispatch stated that those around President Hoover were greatly moved by the British note. A certain important figure said that if the authorities had constitutional authority and political power, then Britain would definitely win. The Christian Century stated that the British note can be regarded as being issued to public opinion, and the response of public sentiment must be awaited in silence. President-elect Roosevelt published an article in the Brooklyn Daily Eagle, stating that debts must be paid. All those with sound judgment should assist debtor nations in all aspects, but canceling debts is both impractical and dishonorable.

Key Figures from Britain, America, and France Gather in Geneva to Reopen Disarmament Talks

U.S. Deputy Representative Hopes the Conference Will Come to a Preliminary Conclusion

Suggests Drafting a Convention Based on Established Principles

To Be Signed by All Representatives, with a Small Group Established to Draft Detailed Rules

Complying with Germany's Demand for Equality

Preparing a So-Called Intermediate Plan

Geneva, 3rd (National News Agency) – After a private conversation this morning between the British and French Prime Ministers, the British Prime Minister met with the Italian representative Aloisi. It is rumored that this afternoon, the three will discuss disarmament issues with the U.S. representative Davis. Herriot is planning to leave Geneva next Tuesday, while MacDonald is expected to stay for a few more days.

Geneva, 3rd (National News Agency) – French Premier Herriot arrived here this morning and will meet with British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon this morning. The so-called intermediate plan to comply with Germany's demand for equality in armaments includes: 1) Allowing Germany to shorten the current term of service for its troops; 2) Allowing these troops to be reorganized according to new standards; 3) Establishing security forces to protect borders and maintain domestic security. At the same time, Germany agrees not to increase its army and navy budget within five years after signing the new disarmament convention. It is rumored that Germany, Italy, and Britain have already approved this plan, but France's attitude is still unclear. If MacDonald and Davis can persuade France to agree as well, it can ensure Germany's return to the disarmament conference and the success of the conference. This matter will likely be decided after German Foreign Minister Neurath arrives here early next week.

Geneva, 2nd (Havas) – Before the reopening of the disarmament conference, political talks have already begun today. However, all we know is that British Prime Minister MacDonald met with U.S. representative Davis in the morning and with French representative Paul-Boncour in the afternoon. According to the views of American personnel participating in the disarmament conference, the intention of the U.S. representative is to urgently seek a concrete result. The claim that they hope for the failure of disarmament is far from the truth. The U.S. side believes that the disarmament conference has reached the stage of drafting a preliminary convention because the disarmament conference has already passed several principles. Major countries can promote this convention based on them. As for the resolution adopted by the disarmament conference on July 23rd, it seems insufficient. All parties may immediately agree to first draft a treaty with a limited scope and important nature, without urgently seeking a complete solution to the issues of disarmament and security. American personnel hope that a preliminary result can be obtained before Christmas.

Geneva, 2nd (Reuters) – An American spokesperson here said today that the general public is becoming weary of the lack of progress at the Disarmament Conference. In order to stir up excitement, the United States has suggested that the methods agreed upon by the Disarmament Conference during its nine-month meeting be compiled into a convention to be signed by all sixty countries attending Geneva. As for the application of this treaty and the completion of detailed rules, they can be handled by the permanent supervisory committee. British Prime Minister MacDonald today initiated talks between the five major powers with U.S. representative Davis and French representative Paul-Boncour, which will determine whether the Disarmament Conference should adopt the American plan or proceed with a larger-scale process.

List of New German Cabinet Members: Chancellor Schleicher Also Serves as Minister of Defense

There are Proposals to Give Hitler a Deputy Chancellor Position

Berlin, 3rd (National News Agency) – This afternoon, new Chancellor General Schleicher submitted the list of cabinet members to the President. The contents have not yet been officially released. It is rumored that Schleicher will concurrently serve as Minister of Defense and Administrative Commissioner of Prussia. Count Krosigk will continue to serve as Minister of Finance, Baron von Rübenach will continue to serve as Minister of Transportation, Dr. Gürtner will serve as Minister of Justice, and Dr. Popitz will serve as Acting Administrative Commissioner of Prussia as a minister without portfolio. In the afternoon, the old cabinet held a meeting, followed by an informal meeting of the ministers remaining in office. It is expected that the new cabinet will be sworn in this afternoon and then immediately consider urgent issues related to Foreign Minister Neurath's trip to Geneva.

Berlin, 2nd (National News Agency) – The new German Chancellor, General Schleicher, is currently fifty years old. He comes from one of the oldest families in Germany, known for their military achievements for generations. Therefore, Schleicher joined the army at the age of seventeen and rose through the ranks rapidly. At the age of forty-six, he had already reached the rank of general, which is the youngest general in German history. During the European War, Schleicher served in the Railway Department directly under the General Staff. After the war, he joined the National Defense Force and soon became the most trusted person of Defense Minister Groener. When the Brüning cabinet resigned, Schleicher was appointed Minister of Defense, having gained the trust of President Hindenburg. Although Schleicher held the position of Director of National Defense in the Papen cabinet, his actual importance exceeded his title because the National Socialist Party was gaining momentum and seeking to seize power by force. General Schleicher showed no weakness towards them, and Hitler's ambition ultimately failed to succeed.

Berlin, 2nd (Reuters) – New Chancellor Schleicher is currently engaged in organizing a new cabinet. Schleicher intends to abandon former Chancellor Papen's plan to amend the constitution and abolish the wage reduction order opposed by the Social Democratic Party. This atmosphere of avoiding conflict with the parliament is considered good, and Schleicher is seen as an eccentric in German politics. The new chancellor, with the assistance of Dr. Luther of the German Bank, will draft a program on economy and unemployment. It is expected that this program can be agreed upon by all parties. Schleicher is also trying to win over Hitler of the National Socialist Party, possibly giving him the position of Deputy Chancellor. It is rumored that Schleicher's appointment as Chancellor was not what President Hindenburg wanted. The President still wanted Papen to govern, but Papen knew that some of the original cabinet members were unwilling to join his new cabinet, so he declined the position and recommended Schleicher to replace him, as he would be more compatible with the parliament. The new government will meet with the parliament on Tuesday, at which time the parliament may extend the session by one week to allow for negotiations between the party leaders.

Indian Round Table Conference Discusses Defense Issues

Governor-General Retains Administrative Privileges

Irwin's Remarks Face Criticism

London, 2nd (Reuters) – The Indian Round Table Conference has resolved constitutional issues such as suffrage. The second week of consideration is largely focused on the central government assuming responsibility from the beginning to the completion of self-government, and the safeguards during the transition period. Former Viceroy Irwin expressed the British government's opinion, stating that in addition to managing national defense and foreign relations, the Governor-General should have the power to find ways to maintain peace, protect minorities, protect the rights of the Indian states, and protect relations with other parts of the British Empire. After three days of debate, Indian Secretary of State Hoare, representing the government, explained that these privileges should be implemented in a limited manner to avoid hindering responsibility. There was much criticism of the layer protecting the British Empire's relations. Hoare claimed that this did not mean that the Governor-General could interfere in normal times between the Indian government and other self-governing governments, but that the protection would only be used when relations were tense and jeopardized the integrity of the Empire's government. Now that there is opposition, he will reconsider it. Hoare concluded with an optimistic statement, saying that there is more hope now than at the beginning of the meeting.

Persia Celebrates the Recovery of Oil Rights

Russian Newspaper Praises It as a Courageous Act

Tehran, 2nd (Reuters) – The Persian government's cancellation of the D'Arcy oil concession has been approved by the parliament today. The city is still celebrating this move. All shops are decorated with lights and lanterns. People are riding in vehicles through the city in teams, singing along the way. All theaters are free of charge. Other cities in Persia have also held celebrations upon receiving the news. The Anglo-Persian Oil Company has announced that it is currently drafting a report to be submitted to shareholders and will be published soon. It is noted that the Persian government announced the cancellation of this concession on November 30 because it was granted before Persia had a constitutional government, so its terms should be renegotiated, but the Anglo-Persian Oil Company ignored it. The British authorities are now paying close attention to this matter because the British hold a large number of shares in the Anglo-Persian Oil Company and because its oil is supplied to the British Navy.

Moscow, 2nd (TASS) – The Soviet government gazette "Izvestia" stated in an editorial today that the Persian government's cancellation of the Anglo-Persian Oil Company concession is a major political event. The newspaper briefly described how the Persian government opposed the company's use of special accounting methods to reduce paper profits, preventing the Persian government from obtaining its share as stipulated in the agreement, referring to this method as "one of the most sinister forms of imperialist colonial plunder." It also said that the solution to this problem must be found outside of legal methods because this move is a political event. The British government will not only use its position in the world oil industry, but will also use all the political and military power of the Empire to overwhelm the Persian government. Therefore, the Persian government's recovery of oil rights can be described as an act of great courage. The newspaper concluded that "The Persian government's daring to take this action is also because the British Empire has lost its world leadership position under the world economic panic. No matter what the outcome of future negotiations, this move shows a sign of the breakdown of British colonial policy, and its impact on Eastern countries will further shake the foundation of the British Empire."

Italy and Japan Build New Warships Amid Disarmament Talks

Rome, 2nd (Reuters) – Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has ordered the construction of two new cruisers, each weighing 7,000 tons, and two torpedo boats. This is part of the 30,000-ton warship construction program for 1932-33 approved by the Italian government this summer.

Yokosuka, 3rd (Den-tsu) – The first-class destroyer "Nenohi" (1,200 tons), which is being built at the Uraga Dock, is nearing completion. The Yokosuka Naval District Commander will be present on the 22nd to hold a grand launching ceremony.

War Damage Suffered by the People of Sichuan

Battles in Jiangjin, Luzhou, Zizhong, and Chengdu

More than 3,000 Innocent People Died

Commercial Losses in Chengdu, Chongqing, and Various Counties in the War Zone Total Approximately 70 Million

Chongqing Correspondence - Two months have passed since the outbreak of the Sichuan war. The generally brave and combative warlords are now exhausted, with both men and horses panting, and the intensity is not as great as before. There is a general feeling that this may come to an end and a temporary ceasefire may be called. As a result, there has been a glimmer of hope in the vast future of the Sichuan situation, and the call for peace is rising. However, the spring spirit is just beginning to unfold, and changes are unpredictable. It is still impossible to predict what the future situation will be. However, it is necessary to describe the conditions of the various armies after the war and the suffering endured by the common people. In this Sichuan war, the Allied forces had a large momentum and would naturally gain the upper hand. However, the losses were also quite significant. Taking Liu Xiang's 21st Army, which is said to have land, sea, and air power, as an example, the number of soldiers who died was very large. In total, there were five regimental commanders, fifteen battalion commanders, and more than one hundred company and platoon commanders. More than 11,000 soldiers were wounded or killed. Two aircraft were destroyed, and two warships were destroyed. Military spending amounted to about 8 million. The benefits gained were the incorporation of Deng Guozhang's independent brigade, Tian Guanwu's fourth brigade, Yang Shangyuan's fifth brigade of the 24th Army, and Hou Zhi's Qian army division, totaling about 15,000 people. In addition, it seized 20 counties from the 24th Army, including Jiangjin, Yongchuan, Dazu, Jinan, Rongchang, Longchang, Neijiang, Fushun, Luxian, Xuyong, Weiyuan, Hejiang, Naxi, Nanxi, Gusong, Gulan, Jianwei, Yangxian, Rongxian, and Jiang'an. Among them, Fushun's salt well tax, which reaches 40 to 50 million yuan per year, is jointly extracted by Liu and the Allied forces and is the most prosperous. As for Yang Sen, the commander of the 20th Army of the Allied forces, Li Jiayu of the New Sixth Division, and Luo Zezhou of the 23rd Division, they jointly attacked the 24th Army, occupied Shunqing, and reached Jianyang. A total of four regimental commanders, thirty-eight battalion, company, and platoon commanders, and more than 2,500 soldiers died. They incorporated about ten companies from Liu Wenhui's troops and occupied six counties in the 24th Army's defense area: Shunqing, Suining, Anyue, Lezhi, Lanyang, and Zizhong. As for Tian Songyao of the 29th Army and Deng Xihou of the 28th Army from the provincial side, after joining the war, they fiercely attacked Liu Wenhui in the Chengdu area, resulting in unprecedented street fighting. About 2,700 people were killed in the two departments. Diao Wenjun, the brigade commander of Deng's department, was also killed.

Page 10

Killed. Many state-owned company and platoon commanders died. Deng occupied Liu Wenhui's defense area, including Chongqing, Shuangliu, and Renshou counties. Deng and Tian both withdrew from Chengdu. Tian even lost the arsenal. In the Allied forces, they were considered to have suffered a significant loss. In addition, the Sichuan army without benefits and losses was only Liu Cunhou's part of the Sichuan-Shaanxi army. Liu is the oldest in qualifications among Sichuan military officers. This time, he joined the anti-Liu campaign as a figurehead of the Allied forces. As for the 24th Army of Liu Wenhui, which was surrounded by enemies and suffered the greatest losses, having lost more than 20 counties of defense area and wasted more than 25,000 troops, they are still strong and unwilling to submit, and have the intention of making a desperate bet to determine the final victory. Currently, Deputy Commander Xiang Yuren is promoting the old tune of the Baoding system unity, and Deng, Tian, and Liu are still cooperating and are brewing in progress. Whether it can be successful is still a question. The losses of the Allied and Liu's forces in this war were limited. The most affected were the common people. In the Jiangjin campaign, the 21st Army bombed Liu Wenhui's troops. Aircraft dropped bombs in the city, killing more than 200 civilians. The Luzhou campaign was even bigger, with more than 1,000 people killed. In the Zizhong campaign, 200 to 300 people also died. The Chengdu area was even bigger. In the Meishan campaign, 700 to 800 people died. In total, no less than 3,000 people died. According to commercial investigations, the commercial losses in Chengdu, Chongqing, and various counties in the war zone affected by the war totaled more than 70 million. I do not know why the Sichuan warlords would bestow this gift on the people. (November 30)

Investigation of Mao and Wang's Power in the Guizhou Crisis

Guizhou's Military Strength Totals Approximately 30,000

Half Supporting Mao, Half Supporting Wang

Victory or Defeat Depends on Reinforcements

Chongqing Air Dispatch: Since the battle between Guizhou Province and Xicheng and Li Yao, more than a year has passed, and the elite troops of each department have been almost completely lost. After Zhou's death, Mao Guangxiang succeeded Zhou Wan in both military and civil administration. The total military strength of the province is four divisions and three independent brigades, including Mao Guangxiang, the commander of the 25th Army and concurrent director of the Training Division; Wang Jialie, the commander of the First Division and concurrent deputy army commander; You Guocai, the commander of the Second Division; Jiang Zaizhen, the commander of the Third Division; Hou Zidan, the commander of the First Independent Brigade; Che Mingyi, the commander of the Second Independent Brigade; and Yi Huaizhi, the commander of the Third Independent Brigade. Mao is stationed in Guiyang, Wang is stationed in Hongjiang in western Hunan, You is stationed in Anshun in the western district, Jiang is stationed in Zunyi in the northern district, Hou is stationed in Chishui in the northern district, Yi is stationed in Bijie in the western district, and Che is stationed in Tongren in the eastern district. Last year, Wang Jialie returned to Guizhou from Hunan and forced Mao to step down. He then greatly reorganized his troops. In addition to the original military strength, he also expanded his troops with 4,000 German rifles obtained from the central government. Wang Jialie now serves as the commander of the 25th Army and concurrently as the director of the Training Division; He Zhizhong is the commander of the First Division; You Guocai is the commander of the Second Division and concurrent deputy army commander; Jiang Zaizhen is the commander of the Third Division; Hou Zidan is the commander of the Fourth Division; Che Mingyi is the commander of the Fifth Division; Song Xing is the commander of the First Independent Brigade; Lan Wenbo is the commander of the Second Independent Brigade; Li Chengzhang is the commander of the Third Independent Brigade; and You Yujiu is the commander of the Fourth Independent Brigade. As for the current locations of each army, Wang Jialie is stationed in Guiyang with approximately three regiments of the Training Division, equipped with 4,000 rifles. The head of the military officer training regiment is Wang himself, with more than 1,300 students and 1,300 rifles. The military police battalion has more than 500 men and rifles, and the guard battalion has 500 men, including a pistol company, a "hook hook" rifle company, a light machine gun company, and a carbine company. The Special Forces Training Center has an artillery battalion with 16 field guns, 600 rifles, and 36 machine guns. He Zhizhong is stationed in Xiangjiang with three regiments and approximately 3,500 men and rifles. You Guocai, commander of the Second Division, is stationed in Anshun, Guizhou, with three regiments and approximately 3,300 men and rifles. Jiang Zaizhen, commander of the Third Division, is stationed in Zunyi, northern Guizhou, with two regiments and another battalion, totaling over 1,500 men and rifles. Jiang has also incorporated bandits from Sichuan and Guizhou, totaling approximately 1,000 men and rifles, led by Li Derong, Yang Qichang, and Shuangqing. Hou Zidan, commander of the Fourth Division, is stationed in Chishui, northern Guizhou, and currently serves as the commander of the 21st Army of the Sichuan-Guizhou Border Defense, with three regiments and approximately 3,000 men and rifles. Che Mingyi, commander of the Fifth Division, is stationed in Tongren, eastern Guizhou, with three regiments and approximately 2,000 men and rifles. Song Xing, commander of the First Independent Brigade, is stationed in Bijie, western Guizhou, with two regiments and approximately 2,000 men and rifles. Jian Wenbo, commander of the Second Independent Brigade, has three regiments with approximately 1,000 men and rifles and is currently stationed in northern Guizhou. Li Chengzhang, commander of the Third Independent Brigade, has two regiments stationed in Guiyang with over 1,600 men and rifles. You Yujiu, commander of the Fourth Independent Brigade, is stationed in Guiyang with two regiments and approximately 1,500 men and rifles. In recent days, Wang Jialie has felt uneasy because of the strong influence of You, Hou, Jiang, Che, and others, who are not directly under his command. Although Mao Guangxiang nominally holds the title of Commander-in-Chief of the Eighteen Routes after stepping down, You, Jiang, and others are quite close to him. Wang is deeply afraid of a joint action against him and will be difficult to deal with. Therefore, he advocated that military expenditures are insufficient and that the troops must be reduced in size, uniformly abolishing divisions and turning them into brigades, in order to reduce the strength of Jiang and others. You, Jiang, and others have long been dissatisfied with Wang's preferential treatment of troops directly under his command. After the plan to reduce troops was leaked, it aroused strong opposition. Mao Guangxiang seized the opportunity to vigorously incite the generals, who had excellent personal relations with Mao. Naturally, they hit it off, leading to the current scene of supporting Mao and overthrowing Wang. The generals of the Mao faction are You Guocai, Hou Zidan, Jiang Zaizhen, Che Mingyi, Song Xing, You Yujiu, etc., with a total of approximately 15,000 troops. The rest who support Wang include He Zhizhong, Li Chengzhang, Jian Fangbo, the Training Division, and the Military Officer Training Regiment, with approximately 14,000 troops. The strength of both sides is equal, but Mao Guangxiang has stronger reinforcements. Jiang Zaizhen, commander of the Third Division, who most strongly supports Mao, took the lead in Zunyi, deploying troops on the Wujiang River to threaten Wang and sending the Zhang Binglin regiment of that division to attack the Lan Wenbo brigade of Wang's army. Fierce battles took place between the two sides on the 18th and 19th in Xinchang, Matashi, Shuangchongyan, and other places near the Wujiang River. Che Mingyi's division also moved from Tongren and has arrived in Meitan. As for You Guocai, he led his troops straight to Guiyang on the 26th. Wang Jialie was caught off guard and withdrew in a hurry, concentrating near Guiyang. After You entered Guiyang, he sent a telegram to welcome Mao back to office. Mao also set off from Zunyi to go to Guiyang. The Guizhou coup seems to have come to an end on the surface, but Wang Jialie's strength has not been significantly depleted and still concentrates near the provincial capital. It is feared that war will still be difficult to avoid. (November 30th)

Chiang Kai-shek Sends Personnel to Investigate and Prohibit Opium Cultivation in Ten Provinces

Measures are Formulated and Submitted to the National Government for Filing

And Ordered the Chairmen of the Ten Provincial Governments to Comply

Hankou Dispatch: In order to strictly prohibit opium and eradicate poisonous plants, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek decided to send personnel to Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hubei, Hunan, Henan, Jiangxi, Fujian, Shaanxi, and Gansu to supervise and prohibit opium cultivation. He also formulated nine articles of the "Measures for Sending Personnel to Investigate and Prohibit Opium Cultivation in Ten Provinces," which were submitted to the National Government for filing on December 1, and telegraphed to the chairmen of the above-mentioned provincial governments to comply. The original submission and measures are recorded as follows:

Submission

The harm of opium is the most severe, and it has been strictly prohibited for years. In recent years, the provinces have followed each other, privately planting it, and there is no way to control it. Poisonous plants are everywhere, and provinces that did not previously cultivate opium, such as Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Henan, also have it everywhere, and it is spreading more and more. This year, while I, Chiang Kai-shek, was leading troops to suppress bandits and going up the Yangtze River, what I saw and heard made me feel even more heartbroken. The reason for this is that a few soldiers and officials have condoned and sheltered it, which is undeniable. As for evil people and treacherous merchants, who are greedy for profit and forget righteousness, they privately traffic and sell opium, and even transform it into morphine and other anesthetic products, making red and white poisonous pills and secretly selling them throughout the country. If we do not seek a fundamental way to eradicate it, there will be a lot of hard work in allowing it to grow. I have now formulated nine articles of the Measures for Sending Personnel to Investigate and Prohibit Opium Cultivation in Ten Provinces. I will select capable personnel and send them to various provinces to supervise the local military and civilian leaders in strictly investigating and prohibiting opium cultivation, starting with the provinces in the interior to eradicate the roots of poisonous plants, and then moving on to others. All the formulated Measures for Sending Personnel to Investigate and Prohibit Opium Cultivation in Ten Provinces, and the reasons for sending personnel to supervise and investigate, are hereby submitted to the National Government for review and filing. This submission is made to the National Government.

Measures

Respectfully presented to the chairmen of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hubei, Hunan, Henan, Jiangxi, Fujian, Shaanxi, and Gansu: The Measures for Sending Personnel to Investigate and Prohibit Opium Cultivation in Ten Provinces are hereby formulated. (Article 1) The ten provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hubei, Hunan, Henan, Jiangxi, Fujian, Shaanxi, and Gansu should first prohibit the cultivation of opium, which shall be the responsibility of the military and civilian leaders of each province. In order to promote efficiency, the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission shall appoint a special commissioner for investigation and prohibition and a number of commissioners for prohibition to go to each province to supervise and prohibit opium cultivation. For the convenience of handling affairs, the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission may directly appoint the aforementioned personnel from the Bandit Suppression Headquarters, which he concurrently leads. (Article 2) The investigation and prohibition shall be divided into two phases. The first phase shall be when planting is approaching, and the second phase shall be when the opium seedlings emerge from the soil. At that time, the special commissioner for investigation and prohibition shall, together with the provincial government, select commissioners or committee members to go to each county with opium seedlings to earnestly handle the matter. (Article 3) When the first phase, when planting is approaching, each county with opium shall send one committee member, or several counties shall send one committee member. Their tasks are as follows: (1) Together with the county government, supervise the heads of each district, township, and village and the heads of the Baojia system to carefully investigate within their jurisdiction. If poppy seeds are found, they shall be confiscated immediately. Those who plant them and refuse to comply shall be detained and sent to be dealt with according to the law. (2) Together with the county government and local party departments, legal groups, etc., carry out publicity and lectures in the public offices of each district, town, and township to enable the people to understand the harm of opium and the severity of national laws, and to voluntarily switch to planting food crops. (3) After the committee members have completed the inspection in the county, they shall, together with the county magistrate, summon all the heads of each district, township, and village and the heads of the Baojia system, and instruct them to personally go to or send people to patrol within their jurisdiction at any time, and order them to submit a written guarantee that opium seedlings will never be found in the future. (Article 4) When the second phase, when opium seedlings emerge from the soil, each county with opium seedlings shall send one committee member. Their tasks are as follows: (1) Together with the county magistrate, personally go to each township for spot checks and supervise the heads of each district, township, and village and the heads of the Baojia system to carefully inspect. If opium seedlings are found, they shall be eradicated immediately, and the planters shall be detained and sent to be dealt with according to the law. (2) If the people in the bandit areas are accustomed to their old habits and greedily plant opium, which cannot be reached by the heads of the district, township, and village and the heads of the Baojia system, they shall consult with the county magistrate and ask the troops stationed in the county to lead the police and other teams to eradicate the opium, but they shall not use this as an excuse to cause trouble. (3) Remote areas are prone to secret planting, and the heads of the district, township, and village and the heads of the Baojia system are not completely honest. They must be diligently investigated, and more attention must be paid to the concealment by the heads of the district, township, and village and the heads of the Baojia system. (Article 5) The committee members shall report the investigation and prohibition situation to the provincial government and the special commissioner for investigation and prohibition once every ten days. (Article 6) If the troops stationed in each county and the local gentry dare to protect opium cultivation, causing the county magistrate to be unable to perform his duties and the committee members to be unable to complete their tasks, the committee members shall secretly report to the special commissioner for investigation and prohibition, who shall consult with the military and civilian leaders of the province to investigate and deal with them strictly according to the law. If the circumstances are serious, the special commissioner for investigation and prohibition may report to the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission for review. (Article 7) The special commissioner for investigation and prohibition shall investigate the situation in each county at any time. If there are places where private planting has been prevalent for years and where the customs are strong and the people are not afraid of the law, he shall designate commissioners or go there himself to handle the matter. (Article 8) If the military and civilian leaders of each province and the county magistrates of each county dare to neglect the matter of prohibiting opium cultivation or openly disobey and secretly condone it, the special commissioner for investigation and prohibition shall secretly report to the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission for review and strict punishment. If the special commissioner for investigation and prohibition and the commissioners for prohibition fail to carry out the investigation and prohibition effectively, intentionally perfunctorily, or report untruthfully, they shall be severely punished once they are found out. (Article 9) These measures shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. Seal of Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission and Commander-in-Chief of the Bandit Suppression of the Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Provinces. (December 1)

Guangdong Troops Repel Communist Bandits on the Fujian Border

Communist Bandits Invading Wuping Were Defeated by the Huang Division

The Communist Bandits Did Not Dare to Invade Xinfeng Because of Strong Military Strength

Guangzhou Dispatch: Recently, the troops of various routes in Guangdong have been searching for Communist bandits in eastern Jiangxi. However, the Communist bandits have recently disintegrated into smaller units and are operating in various places in southeastern and western Jiangxi, attacking where the defense troops are lax. Near Anyuan, hundreds of Communist bandits were recently discovered at Wangmu Ferry, planning to attack the county seat of Xinfeng. The local defense troops of the Wang Zanbin Division immediately prepared for defense and telegraphed friendly troops for reinforcements. Therefore, there were rumors that the Guangxi troops would transfer the Zhou Zuhuang Division to Xinfeng, but this has not yet been implemented, presumably because the issues of military pay and transit have not yet been resolved. Although the Guangxi troops have not moved at this time, for the sake of mutual dependence, the Guangdong troops in southern Jiangxi have dispatched two routes to assist in the defense near Xinfeng. A part of the Fourth Division of the Second Army of San'nan has gone north, and the Second Division of the First Army has also come east from Nankang. The Third Independent Division has come from Nanxiong to Wuqing and other places, so the area of Xinfeng is still safe at this time. The Communist bandits, seeing that Xinfeng has superior military strength, changed their plans and fled back to eastern Jiangxi to attack Shanghang and Wuping on the Fujian border. On the 23rd of this month, more than 300 bandits invaded the county seat of Wuping. Upon receiving the report, the Guangdong troops of the First Independent Division immediately sent the Huang Battalion of the Fifth Regiment to intercept them, killing and wounding many Communist bandits and seizing many red flags. Yesterday, Division Commander Huang telegraphed a report on the defeat of the bandits as follows: "At dawn on the 23rd, the Huang Battalion Commander Dao Ren of the Fifth Regiment was dispatched to lead a team to guerrilla in Shanghang and other places. At Shuikou, Shanghang, they encountered the Luo Guibo and Lai Qinghu units of the pseudo-Independent Third Division and the pseudo-Guerrilla Team, with approximately 300 Communist bandits and two water-cooled machine guns. The bandits resisted from a high position. After fighting for about two hours, the bandits were unable to withstand it and fled in disarray towards Wu She and Chizhu Ridge. We immediately pursued them. By the time we reached Lei Ren She, it was already late and the mountain roads were rugged, so we had to lead the team back to Shanghang for the night. It was found that the bandits had planned to attack the county seat of Wuping, but they were severely suppressed by us. It is estimated that in this battle, more than ten bandits were killed and more than twenty were wounded. We continued to search and suppress the bandits in Chizhu Ridge and Longxi on the morning of the 24th. Further details will be reported later. Respectfully submitted by Huang Renhuan." (November 26)

Those in Charge of Drug Manufacturing Were All Well-Known People

Han Traitor Yu Chonghan Assassinated

Assassinated While Under the Strict Guard of Japanese Soldiers

The Assassin Was a Puppet Official Who Has Not Yet Been Apprehended

A Glimpse of the Chaotic Situation in the Puppet State

The World Society translates the Miller Review as saying that the infighting and conspiracies within the Japanese puppet "Manchukuo" have been confirmed by the assassination of Yu Chonghan (pseudo-President of the Privy Council). Regarding this matter, some small newspapers in Shanghai have mentioned it briefly, but no details have been announced elsewhere in the Far East. The only record of this assassination case appears to be in the October 24th issue of the New York Times Magazine. Although the names recorded in that magazine are not accurate, the details of the case are apparently correct, as a reader of the Miller Review living in Dalian has now sent a similar report on the case. It is not known where the New York Times Magazine got this information, but the name of the restaurant where the case occurred is apparently mixed up with the name of the victim, Yu Chonghan. According to the magazine, Yu Chonghan was eating in a Chinese restaurant in the Japanese railway district of Changchun, heavily guarded by Japanese police. Suddenly, another official of the puppet Privy Council named Li Yisheng (transliteration) broke in. Li had apparently once served as the Civil Affairs Director of Heilongjiang Province, but was later dismissed. The magazine's account also mentions another official from Qiqihar named Cheng Zhiyuan (transliteration, according to the report, Cheng was shot by General Tamon, commander of the 2nd Japanese Division; yesterday's news said that Cheng was a pseudo-acting governor of Heilongjiang Province), who was said to have been dismissed due to Yu Chonghan's conspiracy. Therefore, it is not clear who masterminded this case. What is known is that Yu Chonghan, a high-ranking official of "Manchukuo" serving under the Japanese, was assassinated, and the assassin was another Chinese official, who has not yet been arrested or brought to justice. As mentioned earlier, Yu was eating in a restaurant under the protection of Japanese guards when another Chinese official broke in (seized a butcher knife used in the kitchen, and stabbed Yu in the head and neck in multiple places). Yu later died of his injuries in the Mantetsu Hospital in Dalian on November 1. At the time, the assassin, seeing that his purpose had been achieved, simply walked out of the restaurant and into another restaurant to eat. The Japanese police authorities turned a blind eye and did not arrest him. Since then, the case has been issued by the Japanese authorities to immediately implement censorship, so the matter was not recorded in newspapers in Manchuria and Japan. Only the English-language Japanese Record newspaper (run by the British, carried only briefly, and did not mention his name, but speculated that the murderer will be subject to legal punishment, is the only account), even the news of Yu's death in a Dalian hospital was censored, so the news released by the United Press of America from a Japanese telegram also contains mixed messages.

The assassination of Yu Chonghan and the failure of the Japanese to bring Yu's murderer to justice provide us with an interesting glimpse into the current situation in the puppet capital. A foreigner familiar with world affairs who recently traveled to Changchun claimed that, in his view, the current state of the capital of "Manchukuo" is unlike that of any other capital in the world. The Japanese's promotion of "Manchukuo" as "solid" is contrary to reality. The Japanese never trust anyone. Any Chinese official working with the Japanese is at risk of being assassinated. After the September 18th Incident in Shenyang last year, Yuan Jinkai, who helped the Japanese organize the Shenyang Public Security Maintenance Association, told the League of Nations Investigation Commission that he was in danger of being assassinated and was constantly under the surveillance of Japanese military police. Therefore, Yu Chonghan's assassination is all the more illustrative of how chaotic and dark the situation is in "Manchukuo" under Japanese control.

On the night of the 10th, the team was dispatched to search the homes and shops of the above-mentioned criminals. It turned out that after the manufacturing site in Zhangjiazhai was uncovered, some of the criminals had already absconded. As a result, Cao Ziting and Jiang Zhankui were arrested. Cao Huiwu and Zhou Wangshi were arrested at Zhou Jingchang's home. Wen Zichengxiang, Wen Shishi, and Wen Zhangshi were arrested at Wen Shaoshan's home. Ding Zizhaofeng and the suspect Zhou Yuhan were arrested at Ding Yinzhou's business. Wang Ruiqin, a partner of the Daguanyuan, was also arrested. The others had already fled far away. These criminals were all escorted to the Garrison Headquarters and questioned separately. The Garrison Headquarters is still considering how to handle this case, and there are probably two options: one is to present a request for execution by shooting in accordance with military law, and the other is to publicly impose a heavy fine and use the funds for local public welfare. It is also planned to solicit local opinions to make a decision. It is also heard that this drug manufacturing organization was initially established in the station area, in the home of a certain criminal, and moved several times, eventually reaching Zhangjiazhai. One drug manufacturing machine was destroyed at the time, and the remaining are now stored in the Garrison Headquarters. Criminal Cao already has white hair and a silver beard, and is over sixty years old. The other criminals are also quite wealthy, but they still engaged in this illegal act, which must be severely punished. (December 2)

Songjiang Bran Cake Industry Asks for Reduction of Business Tax

The Songjiang Fengjing Town Bran Cake and Bean Cake Industry Association, because the Department of Finance collects business tax in accordance with the grain tax, which is unbearable, has telegraphed again to the Department of Finance to request a reduction. The original telegram is as follows: "Respectfully presented to Director Shu of the Zhenjiang Department of Finance. Regarding the request to exempt the bran cake industry from increasing business tax, it has been telegraphed to your office some days ago. Now, we have received a reply stating that, upon reviewing the temporary regulations on business tax in Jiangsu Province, the grain industry in the attached tax rate table is subject to business tax at a reduced tax rate of 0.5%. Since the bran cake industry is a kind of grain, it should be taxed at the grain industry tax rate without any doubt. As for rice and flour, which are the main products in grain, the government has made a special accommodation for the sake of emphasizing people's livelihood, and the temporary tax rate is still 0.2%. No other industries may cite this as an example. The request that the bran cake industry maintain the original tax amount should not be granted. Upon receiving this, we found that the two words 'grain' refer to those that can be eaten, such as rice, millet, sorghum, wheat, etc. The grain tax certificates issued by your department over the years have also not included the bran cake industry. It is very obvious that bran cake should not be considered a kind of grain. The reply stating that the bran cake industry is a kind of grain is purely a misunderstanding. Moreover, bran cake is a necessary item for farmers' cultivation. Without bran cake, even if they can cultivate, how can the fields be fertile? If the fields are not fertile, how can there be a harvest? If there is no harvest, it will inevitably affect people's livelihood. The situation is important and more urgent than rice and flour among grains. The tax rate should be even lower than the tax rate of rice and flour among grains, in order to comply with the government's intention to take care of people's livelihood. We humbly implore your department to consider the decline in commerce and the suffering of people's livelihood, maintain the original tax, and do not increase it. We await your orders with utmost anxiety. respectfully submitted by the Songjiang Fengjing Town Bran Cake and Bean Cake Industry Association."

Ministry's Approval of the Case of Boundary Demarcation Between Fengxian and Fengnan

Regarding the case of boundary demarcation between Fengnan, the standing committee member of the county party department, Jiang Wenhe, submitted to the Ministry of Interior a reply stating: "According to the Chief of the Civil Affairs Department of this ministry, the special commissioner for inspecting local administration and local autonomy in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, Wang Xianqiang, signed a report stating that the committee member and others had submitted a request to transfer the 15 townships including Taiping in Nanhui County to the jurisdiction of Fengxian County. Red Pills Permeate Various Counties in Huaihai

The area north of the Yangtze River in Jiangsu Province is located in a remote area, and the folk customs are still considered simple and honest. Social evils are self-disciplined and strict. However, in recent years, opium has deeply penetrated the people, and Red Pills, which are a hundred times more harmful than opium, have also gradually spread to various counties in Huaihai. According to investigations, the total value of Red Pills imported into various counties in Huaihai each year has reached more than 5 million yuan. The authorities' eyes and ears are not comprehensive, and prohibitions are ineffective. Smokers smoke, vendors sell, and manufacturers produce without any scruples. Red Pills have deeply penetrated the people in northern Jiangsu, causing endless harm. According to recent investigations, in each larger village and town in the Huaihai counties, more than ten yuan worth of Red Pills can be sold per day. Based on ten villages per district, more than one hundred yuan can be sold per day. This refers to the general laborers, coolies, and vagrants in society. The wealthy sons and daughters, who have larger addictions and smoke four or five to seven or eight yuan a day, are not included. In summary, the sales of Red Pills in the two Huaihai prefectures are about more than 5 million yuan. Red Pill smokers can be divided into three levels: A. Laborers, coolies, and beggars; B. Farmers and workers; C. Well-to-do young families. The size of their smoking amount increases or decreases depending on the amount of money earned each day. Therefore, the consumption of laborers, coolies, and beggars is relatively limited, unlike wealthy young people who can smoke as much as they want. At present, in the Huaihai area, farmers, workers, and laborers account for 70% of the Red Pill smokers, and well-to-do young sons account for 30%. The original price of each Red Pill can is about ten yuan, but vendors can sell it for more than twenty yuan after reselling. This refers to vendors. If they purchase raw materials and manufacture it themselves, the profits are even greater. Therefore, in the Huaihai area, unscrupulous merchants, wealthy gentry, and magnates who only seek profit consider this to be a shortcut to wealth and flock to it. The Jiangsu Provincial Government has silently observed the hidden evils and has strictly ordered the county magistrates of various counties in northern Jiangsu to strictly prohibit it together to show its determination.

Xu Erxi, the chief prosecutor of the Zhenjiang District Court, has been transferred to the Wuhu County Court. His vacancy will be filled by Liu Xiaokang, who was appointed by the Ministry. Because Liu indicated that he would not take the position, the Ministry of Justice specially transferred Huang Yongzhong, the president of the court, to the position. The vacant position of president will be filled by Hu Yigu, a judge from the Shanghai Court. Mr. Hu is scheduled to come to Zhenjiang next Tuesday to take office. The handover of both the court and the prosecutor's office has been completed and they are waiting for the replacement.

Robbery and Assault Case in the Twelfth District

Zhou Jinxiang, a villager from the 343rd block of the twelfth district of the county, is already in his sixties. His son, Yunxiang, is a farmer. The family is well-off. Around midnight the other night, the whole family had already gone to bed when suddenly seven or eight bandits broke in through the back door. Meeting to Review Local Deficits

The county party department convened a meeting of representatives from various agencies at 2:00 PM on the 1st to review the local financial deficits of the Property Management Office over the years. It was found that the Property Management Office had a listed total deficit of more than 221,400 yuan. After offsetting the 150,000 yuan collected from the 5-cent per mu land tax (excluding education fees), there was still a deficit of more than 71,400 yuan. It is now proposed to include all the outstanding old debts from the 17th and 18th years and the winter grain and reed tax from the 19th and 20th years delivered by the Property Management Office, totaling more than 125,200 yuan, for a total amount of more than 275,200 yuan. Then, according to the precedents of previous years, the actual collection is discounted, so the total amount is 220,000 yuan, which can barely be met. It was decided to submit it to the general meeting for approval and then check the listed arrears. It seems that a comprehensive plan should be made to distinguish between urgent and non-urgent items. It is proposed that the principle of repaying the loans as soon as possible with short-term loans should be adopted. It was decided to suggest that the general meeting adopt it.

Rickshaw Driver Strike Unresolved

There are about 400 rickshaws in this county, and there are also more than 300 privately owned chartered rickshaws. With the decline of commerce, the business of rickshaw drivers has also been greatly affected. They sit on the streets all day, struggling to make a living. However, the rent cannot be missed for even one day. Because of these circumstances, a general strike was unanimously launched starting on the afternoon of the 1st of this month. Except for privately owned chartered rickshaws, rickshaws are nowhere to be seen on the streets. It is reported that their purpose is to request the capitalists to reduce the rent (the rent is 780 cash per day, and now they plan to reduce it to 2 jiao). However, since the Rickshaw Drivers' Union was dissolved this spring, there is no group gathering. The capitalists have no way to contact and resolve the issue for a while. They are currently looking for rickshaw bosses to discuss solutions.

Page 12

The City Government Protests to France and Japan Over the Arrest of Kim Young Duk

Demanding Legal Protection for Chinese Residents Living in Concessions

Kim Recounted Being Brutally Tortured After Being Kidnapped to the Japanese Consulate

Petitioning the City Government to Request Negotiations with the Japanese Side

The Japanese Consulate has Issued an Arrest Warrant, and the French Consulate is Considering It

The city government has protested to both the French and Japanese consulates yesterday afternoon because Japanese plainclothes police have entered the French Concession to arrest people more than once. Kim Young Duk also issued a statement about his arrest. Details are as follows:

City Government Protest

The city government sent protest letters to both the French and Japanese consulates simultaneously at 3:00 PM yesterday. According to the city government's announcement, regarding the case of Japanese consulate plainclothes detectives arbitrarily arresting Kim Young Duk in the French Concession, the city government had already made verbal protests to the French Concession authorities and the Japanese consulate on the day of the incident. Yesterday (3rd), Mayor Wu also sent Secretary Geng Jiaqi to the French Consulate General to submit a written protest, stating that Kim Young Duk is a naturalized Chinese citizen. It is extremely shocking that the French authorities allowed Japanese plainclothes detectives to commit armed robbery and illegally arrest him. Your Excellency, the Consul General, has a responsibility to protect the residents of the concession. Therefore, the occurrence of this incident is deeply regrettable. It is hoped that Your Excellency, the Consul General, will pay close attention to this case so that Chinese citizens residing in the concession can live in peace and enjoy the protection of Chinese law.

The Central News Agency reported that the city government also believes that the illegal arrest of Kim Young Duk, a naturalized Chinese citizen, by Japanese consulate plainclothes detectives is not only an insult to Kim Young Duk personally, but also shows disrespect to the Chinese government by failing to notify the Chinese government in advance. Therefore, the city government also protested to the Japanese consulate yesterday afternoon, demanding an apology from the Japanese consulate and compensation for the losses incurred, and ensuring that similar unfortunate incidents will not occur in the future.

Director Zhang's Statement

According to Zhang Tingrong, director of the City Government Intelligence Office, to a reporter from the Central News Agency, Kim Young Duk's petition for rescue was delivered to the city government the day before yesterday. Kim Young Duk is indeed a naturalized Chinese citizen. Although he has been released after negotiations with the French Consulate, there are a large number of Chinese people residing in the French Concession. The Concession authorities should protect the safety of Chinese people in accordance with Chinese law. Therefore, after Kim Young Duk's petition was delivered to the city government, the city government immediately decided to submit a written protest to the French Consulate to ensure that Chinese people residing in the French Concession can live in peace. However, the initiator of this case was the Japanese side. Therefore, in addition to submitting a written protest to the French side, the city government also submitted a written protest to the Japanese side. The protest letter will be released after it reaches the Japanese consulate.

The Arrest

After his release, Kim Young Duk originally planned to meet with reporters, but due to lack of time, he drafted a document himself to describe his arrest. He said that Huang Zhanying, who claimed to be from Guangdong, introduced a Guangdong revolutionary, Zhou, to his nephew, Kim Cheol, for an appointment at 8:00 PM on the 30th of last month. After Huang and Zhou arrived, they said that a Mr. Li was a friend, so they went out together. After waiting for more than 40 minutes, seven Japanese plainclothes police officers suddenly broke in and took him to a car, which drove to the Japanese consulate. He was taken into a small room, where two Japanese began interrogating him. There was another large room with a large number of armed police officers on guard. The key points of their interrogation focused on two items: 1. The secret addresses of Korean revolutionaries in Shanghai; 2. The accomplices in the bombing cases in Tokyo and Hongkou. He replied that he did not know about these. The Japanese police then subjected him to extreme torture, causing injuries to his head and hands. The interrogation lasted about four hours. The rest was waiting for negotiations. According to Guowen News Agency, Kim has taken his family away from Shanghai to avoid further problems.

Petition to the City Government

Tsai Xiaobai, Kim Young Duk's representative lawyer, submitted a petition to the city government yesterday, stating that the petitioner was entrusted by Kim Young Duk (i.e., Kim Cheol) and Kim Cheol on November 30 to handle negotiations with the French Consulate for his release. Kim Young Duk was also sent to the French Consulate by the Japanese Consulate at about 7:00 PM on the same day and released immediately, entirely due to the vigorous negotiations of Your Excellency's government. After Kim Young Duk was kidnapped to the Japanese Consulate by Japanese plainclothes soldiers, he was subjected to severe torture, and there were injuries to his face and limbs, and many bruises on his waist and back. He is currently residing in the hospital for treatment and will not be able to recover in the shortest possible time. After Kim Young Duk and Kim Cheol became naturalized Chinese citizens in October of the 18th year of the Republic of China, they held Nationality Certificate No. 67 issued by the alliance. The certificate was delivered by the petitioner to the French side for verification. Kim and others are indeed Chinese citizens. This time, the Japanese arbitrarily arrested Chinese citizens without reason and subjected them to torture, disregarding justice and inhumanity, which is deeply hateful. Afterwards, they released him after realizing that they were wrong. Their acknowledgment of illegality has been proven and there is no doubt about it. The matter concerns national rights and people's lives, and is of great importance. Therefore, it is requested that Your Excellency's government immediately lodge a serious protest with the Japanese consulate, demanding a formal written apology and ensuring that similar incidents will not occur in the future. As for the medical expenses for Kim Young Duk's injuries, it is stated that they are reserved. The 560 yuan in banknotes, a gold watch, a fountain pen, a wool coat, and a seal that were searched and taken away by the Japanese detectives should be negotiated for their return so that they can be claimed. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai City Government.

Kim Cheol's Resume

Kim Cheol, courtesy name Young Duk, is 42 years old and has been engaged in revolutionary work for 19 years. He is from Hampyeong, Jeollanam-do, Korea. At the age of 22, he graduated from Dongdae Law College. Indignant at Japan's annexation of Korea, he engaged in the restoration movement. At the age of 23, he left Korea and came to Shanghai to engage in educating Korean children with Korean patriots at sea. After the end of the European War in 1918, he organized the New Korean Youth Party in Shanghai on November 26 of the same year to restore the motherland. Kim served as the party's finance committee chairman. In the same year, he and Dr. Kim Kyu-sik were sent to study in Paris. He secretly returned to Korea and made an agreement with Son Byeong-hee, the leader of Cheondoism, for independence and issued a declaration of independence. Unfortunately, it was unsuccessful. He returned to Shanghai in February 1919, joined comrades, and organized a provisional government. Kim served as the finance committee chairman. The following year, he was transferred to the position of Minister of Transportation. The provisional government was reformed, and he served as Minister of Justice, Minister of Military Affairs, Minister of Finance, and other positions. Three years ago, he formed the Korean Independence Party and served as the director of the party's finance department. He is selfless and righteous, has nationalistic ideas, and is respected by Koreans. However, he has no children and adopted his nephew Kim Cheol as his heir. On October 5th, 28th year of the Republic of China, he became a citizen of the Republic of China and holds Naturalization Certificate No. 67 issued by the Ministry of Interior. Since then, Kim has not participated in Korean revolutionary work for three to five years.

Japanese Side Strictly Pursues

Dalu News reported that the police department of the Japanese Consulate General has filled out two arrest warrants yesterday and sent them to French Consul General Meyrier, requesting the arrest of Kim Cheol and his nephew Kim Cheol. However, it is not yet known what crimes the Japanese side is accusing them of. It is expected that it must be related to political activities. The French Consulate General received the Japanese arrest warrant yesterday afternoon and is still considering it and has not ordered the police to arrest the two.

Police File Suit

The French police have requested the Japanese Consular Court to punish Ainou, Yamazaki, and five other Japanese who fled in a car after arbitrarily arresting Kim on Wednesday. The reply from the Japanese court is currently pending. It is heard that the French police intend to charge the seven with armed kidnapping.

Swearing to Fight to the End as Long as One Breath Remains. Ma is Currently Traveling Indirectly to Zha to Negotiate Everything. General Ma Zhanshan cabled Mr. Zhu Qinglan yesterday, asking him to forward it to various circles in Shanghai, including the statement that he would swear to encourage his troops and fight to the end as long as one breath remained. They have been remitted one after another. The first batch consisted of six payments totaling 21,893 yuan and some cents. The second batch consisted of one payment totaling 70,000 yuan, which was donated by compatriots in Batavia and received by Shi, Mu, Wang, Du, and other gentlemen.
