Li Jingzong Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Aboard Successfully Tested Aircraft

Talks on Successful Test Flight of Northwest Route

Decision to Officially Launch on the 15th of This Month

The Riri News Agency reports that Mr. Li Jingzong, Director of the General Affairs Department of the Ministry of Transportation, returned to Beijing from Ping yesterday afternoon (the 3rd) at 2:30 PM, arriving in Shanghai aboard a test flight aircraft. A reporter from the Riri News Agency paid a special visit to Mr. Li at his private residence yesterday. According to the conversation, Minister of Transportation Zhu Jiahua, recognizing that the northwest is a remote border region adjacent to untrustworthy neighbors, and that its abundant resources are easily coveted, believes that if development is not urgently planned, it will be insufficient to secure the frontier and benefit the border regions. Development, however, requires transportation, so he considers the northwest section of the Eurasian postal transport air route to be necessary to expedite. Furthermore, in view of the postal blockade of the Northeast, Chinese and foreign individuals sending mail to Europe, in order to save time, often fail to appreciate the government's plight, and instead deliver to illegal organizations established by certain parties, hoping to transfer through Siberia to Europe, which results in the outflow of authority. Therefore, expediting the northwest air route to promote the completion of the Eurasian postal transport air route is considered particularly important. However, since the reorganization of the Eurasian Aviation Corporation in June of this year, it has not only repeatedly failed to test the planned routes, but has also almost halted the established routes. Zhu believes that this phenomenon is related to the lack of specialized knowledge, experience, and the ability to manage foreigners on the part of the company's responsible personnel. Therefore, in addition to summoning Mr. Schmidt, the director of the flight crew, to the ministry on the day he took office to personally instruct him, he also appointed himself, as the party who negotiated the Sino-German joint venture Eurasian Aviation Postal Transport contract and the first successful test flight in the northwest, and who is familiar with the Eurasian Aviation Corporation and the northwest situation, to supervise Schmidt and complete the northwest section test flight work by the end of November, in order to prepare for the official launch at the Third Plenary Session. The test flight aircraft arrived in Suzhou on November 18, Hami on the 20th, Dihua on the 21st, Tacheng on the Sino-Russian border on the 25th, flew back to Suzhou on the 29th, Xi'an on the 1st of this month, and Nanjing on the 2nd. Because Zhu had already come to Shanghai on official business on the night of the 1st, he (Li) specially led Schmidt and the aircraft that successfully tested the northwest route to Shanghai today (i.e., yesterday) to report in person and discuss all the preparatory procedures for the official launch on the 15th of this month.

Li Fusun Talks About Observations from Travel in Southeast Asia

Overseas Chinese Enthusiastically Patriotic, Cooperation from All Sectors Is Necessary. Mr. Li Fusun recently gave a speech at the local association on his observations from traveling in Southeast Asia, which is recorded as follows: This trip to Southeast Asia was to send my daughter to Europe to study, and to take the opportunity to inspect the local situation. Furthermore, as I handled the national salvation donations from overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia, I also needed to report to the people there. After arriving in Singapore, I immediately went to Penang, stayed for four days, and was welcomed by the local meeting. I thanked them on behalf of the Shanghai victims. The patriotic enthusiasm of the overseas Chinese is admirable. Although the economic situation has been poor in recent years, it has not diminished their courage to save the country, even among the workers. Those who have become wealthy in Singapore through business often consider Penang as a place to reside for a long time. Their excellent residences all belong to Chinese people. The arrangements in front of the doors are all in the old Chinese style. I often see large lanterns hanging with the name of a certain surname, like the residences of retired officials in the Qing Dynasty. The overseas Chinese there once asked me to whom the national salvation donations should be remitted for proper handling. I replied immediately that it would be most appropriate to remit them to Mr. Zhu Ziqiao for collection and distribution. More than a dozen workers from the labor community there entrusted me with funds to bring back to the motherland and deliver to the receiving agency for relief purposes. Furthermore, the Perak Chamber of Commerce sent representatives to entrust me with tens of thousands of taels of silver for collection and transfer. The overseas Chinese are very concerned about foreign humiliation, and their newspaper propaganda spares no effort. Among the overseas Chinese there, the Hokkien people are the most numerous, followed by the Cantonese. I then went to Singapore, stayed for eight days, and the Chinese Chamber of Commerce and various directors held banquets to welcome me separately. Because I had previously handled the donation of funds, I could not bring the report because it was not yet printed, so I only showed them photos of the Memorial Village and told them about the distribution and usage, which was very satisfying. However, the British Malayan Peninsula (i.e., Singapore, Penang, etc.) has a Chinese Affairs Department, which specializes in Chinese affairs. They are very careful about the nature of Chinese donations. The photos provided further proof and strengthened their trust in the donation for refugee relief. I spoke and met with the Director of Chinese Affairs. The next day, I visited him and explained the donation situation in detail. In Southeast Asia, the industries are tin mining and rubber. Now the price of rubber has fallen. It used to be worth one dollar and eighty-one cents per pound, but now it has fallen to six or seven cents per pound. Workers' lives are becoming increasingly difficult, earning only one or two cents per day, and many rubber plantation owners have gone bankrupt. The number of unemployed workers is increasing. Last year, the local government repatriated about 200,000 unemployed overseas Chinese to their homeland. When sending them back, they provided clothing, food, travel expenses, and a small amount of living expenses. Now they have restricted Chinese immigration. The local government strictly prohibits foreigners from engaging in political activities, saying it easily disrupts commerce. As for the crackdown on Chinese workers, it is actually due to economic decline. The rubber plantations are desolate, and the number of those being sold and mortgaged is unknown. They are now trying to find ways to change the planting to jackfruit and rice. Mr. Chen Jiageng runs a rubber factory, originally to raise funds for Xiamen University, so that Fujian education can be on par with Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Therefore, he is generally respected as a great figure. Mr. Chen is very enthusiastic about using domestic goods and still maintains a worker's attitude. He also described in detail to me that domestic cloth is either not strong enough or the width is narrower, and should be improved. Since the Ottawa Conference, Britain has emphasized protection policies in trade with its territories. The sales of British Southeast Asian products are expected to improve. Overseas Chinese find life easier in the tropics. If the market turns around, their lives can be improved. In the past, overseas Chinese education was not very developed, so the organization was not very sound. Now it has improved slightly. It is reported that in the past, overseas Chinese remitted about 30 million yuan back to China, which is deeply related to the national economy. Therefore, we must cooperate with overseas Chinese to revive the entire national economy. The method of cooperation is to use surplus funds to support overseas Chinese businesses, so that they can be maintained to await a turnaround, and to find ways to promote products, such as rubber and rubber products. As for banking, the banks established by overseas Chinese there are already sufficient to meet the needs, and domestic banks do not need to set up branches there to avoid unnecessary competition. It is estimated that after the September 18th Incident, a total of 2 million yuan was remitted back for donations. If it were during a prosperous market, it would have been 6 to 7 million yuan. Overseas Chinese can be divided into three types: (1) Those who went from China are the most enthusiastic about patriotism; (2) Those who grew up abroad and have returned to China also have enthusiasm; (3) Those who were born locally and have never returned to China inevitably have a weaker attachment to national affairs, which is not surprising. Therefore, the first type of overseas Chinese bears the heaviest burden. Those who wish to return to China to do business, I advise them to continue developing locally, as the Chinese there really account for the greatest effort. The British are very grateful for the Chinese's business efforts. In the past, when it was prosperous, the Singapore municipal government had abundant income, often exceeding the budget. To this day, the municipal treasury still has ample funds, and 80% of the income comes from overseas Chinese. The overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia have such great achievements and a deeply rooted foundation, and are so deeply concerned about the motherland. We must not discriminate against them. Please, Chairman Shi, use the power of newspapers to encourage all sectors to cooperate with overseas Chinese.

A Total of 254 Scout Troops, 1,270 People, Participated

Yesterday was the day of the city's Boy Scouts' general mobilization for aviation mass solicitation. It rained lightly in the afternoon, but the morale of the Scouts was very good, and the discipline was orderly. The requesting students left obediently, which shows that the national salvation movement has penetrated people's hearts. Some troops of Boy Scouts, because the assigned territory was too short, had already walked through it in a short time and requested additional routes, showing their enthusiasm for aviation. At 5:00 PM in the afternoon, the troops successively arrived at the meeting to report on the progress of their work. The results were excellent. The statistics of solicitations for each troop have not yet been compiled and will be disclosed later. It is also heard that the association received letters yesterday from student groups in other cities, such as Nanjing and Hangzhou, responding to the actions of the Shanghai City Boy Scouts, and each held similar events locally, so that the public could understand the true meaning of national salvation.

Swiss Consul Promoted to Chargé d'Affaires in Japan

Will Take Office Next January to Succeed Head of French Consulate in Japan. Mr. A. Daeniker, the current Swiss Consul in Shanghai, has been ordered to be promoted to Chargé d'Affaires in Japan. Mr. Daeniker has been in Shanghai for many years and has served as Acting Consul General for a long time. A reporter from the Central News Agency visited Mr. Daeniker at the Swiss Consulate yesterday and had the following conversation: Question: "You have now been promoted to Chargé d'Affaires in Japan. I wonder who will succeed you as Consul?" Answer: "According to unofficial information, Mr. Hurzeler, the current head of the French Consulate in Japan, will be transferred, but we have not yet received the government's formal instructions." Question: "When will you go to Tokyo to take up your new post?" Answer: "It is currently scheduled for the end of January next year to take office in Japan." Question: "Before you leave China, I wonder what your impression of our country is?" Answer: "I greatly admire your country's culture and philosophy. Two months ago, I traveled to Beiping and passed through Jinan, where I went to Qufu and paid homage to the Confucius Temple. I deeply hope that after the cultural communication between China and the West in the future, it will become increasingly brilliant and great." Question: "The Sino-Japanese dispute is currently being mediated by the League of Nations. From your observation, how will it be resolved in the future?" Answer: "I am not in a position to express my opinion on this point. However, I have learned from the newspapers that all small countries are sincerely supporting the League of Nations Covenant, the Nine-Power Treaty, and the Kellogg-Briand Pact. Therefore, the unfortunate events between China and Japan will be justly and peacefully resolved in the future." Question: "You are now going to Japan. I hope you can convey to the Japanese government and public the Chinese people's love of peace and determination to uphold justice." Answer: "I am very willing to convey to the Japanese government and public the Chinese people's love of peace and determination to uphold justice, and I hope that the friendly relations between China and Japan will become increasingly close."

Record of Inspection of Completed Dike Construction by the National Government Flood Relief Committee (6)

Inspection of the Third District: The Jiangxin steamer set sail at half past twelve. At 4 PM, it arrived at Majiawo and began the inspection of the Third District's engineering. The entire length of the Third District's dike is approximately 281.4 kilometers, with a total of 2,843,292 cubic meters of earthwork completed. The cost was 123,005.59 silver dollars, and the number of disaster relief workers reached 40,125. The area is on the south bank of the Yangtze River, from Fangjia Zhou in Qiupu County to Datong Town, and on the north bank from Zhou Tou Town in Susong County to Liubai Zhang. The Guangji Embankment project is the largest, starting from Zongyang Town, passing through Majiawo and other places, reaching Anqing, with a length of 90 kilometers and a dike width of 8 meters. It provides protection for tens of thousands of mu of farmland within the dike.

Bank Erosion: After arriving at Majiawo, a small boat was hired to reach the north bank to inspect the Guangji Embankment. While in the boat, it was observed that the erosion of mud and sand on the north bank was very rapid, and a gap appeared in an instant. After landing and walking for about a li (half a kilometer), the new dike was reached. The whole way was covered in extremely thick river sand. Walking was like walking on the sand dunes north of the river; the ground sank by an inch with each step, and dust and sand covered the face. The old dike along the river had completely collapsed, and the new dike was also mostly constructed of sand, so it had already subsided by an inch. Although the dike surface was more than twice as wide as usual, due to the easily eroded nature of the sand, it was feared that it would not last long. According to Mr. Xi Dejiong, it was not easy to find a large amount of clay in this area. Although there were light railways and small freight cars, there was still no solution, so it was necessary to mix in sand. The sides of the current dike were made of pure clay, so that it would not be too easily destroyed. The erosion of sand on the riverbank has a huge impact on the dike construction. If no measures are taken to build a drop structure to reduce the force of the water flow, the erosion will continue day and night. After a year, the land along the river will be submerged, not to mention the new dike. This is something that should be given special attention by the government.

Inspection Team of Bandit Areas: Regarding the event where Generalissimo Chiang of the Military Affairs Commission will host the inspection team of bandit areas in four provinces, Xu Shiying, Li Zujun, Wen Lanting, and others, after detailed consultation today, decided to add the entire inspection team. In the afternoon, they telegraphed Chiang, reporting the progress of the organization and hoping that he would send personnel to host them. It was named the Inspection Team for the Temporary Relief and Rehabilitation Association of Bandit Areas in the Henan, Anhui, and Hubei Provinces, led by Xu Shiying. The telegram briefly stated: During this Flood Relief Committee inspection of dike construction, bandits disappeared along the way and residents lived in peace. This shows your great success in suppressing bandits. The representatives are deeply grateful. It is now resolved that the entire group will join the inspection team. Starting today, they will take advantage of the dike construction inspection to also inspect the bandit areas and visit residents suffering from banditry. Upon arrival in Wuhan, they will visit Your Excellency immediately. We respectfully report. Also, after arriving in Anqing, a telegram was sent to Shanghai to report the progress of the organization. (Qian Hua, from Anqing, evening of the 30th).

The Yibin Steamer Catches Fire on the Upper Yangtze

Many Crew Members Injured and Killed; Passengers Fortunately Unharmed. The "Yimao" steamer, belonging to the American-owned Jiejang Company, was en route from Chongqing, Sichuan, back to Shanghai. On the first of this month, while the ship was 35 miles downstream from Yichang, bandits were discovered on the shore. Foreign ships on the upper Yangtze usually have sailors on board for protection, and the ship was equipped with a machine gun in case of emergency. At the time, the bandits first fired shots at the "Yibin," intending to attack. The sailors on board returned fire. Unexpectedly, the bandits switched to using earthen cannons to bombard the ship. The ship was hit by a projectile, and the cannon fire ignited cargo, causing a sudden and fierce fire. The captain ordered the crew and sailors to fight the fire with all their might. Meanwhile, a fast boat was sent to Hankou to avoid the bandit area. It is reported that four or five lower-ranking crew members were injured or suffocated to death while fighting the fire. The ship arrived in Hankou on the 2nd, and the fire had been extinguished. After the Shanghai company learned of this news, they telegraphed Hankou to inquire about the truth of the matter. They also ordered the ship to unload its cargo in Hankou and return to Shanghai for repairs as soon as possible. Fortunately, none of the passengers were injured.

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Telegraphed Request to Strictly Suppress Maritime Bandits

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram to the Executive Yuan and the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces yesterday. On the 2nd of this month, the Shanghai Kerosene Industry Association, a member of the Chamber, sent a letter stating: "Our member, the Guanghua Kerosene Company, informed us that the oil they transport by sailboat to Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces must pass through the Wusongkou (Wusong Port). They were robbed by bandits in the sea near Wusong on three occasions in November of the 19th year of the Republic [1930], and again in April of the 20th year [1931], resulting in a total loss of 60,000 to 70,000 yuan. Although rewards have been offered repeatedly and requests have been made to the naval and land military and police agencies of both provinces to conduct strict investigations and arrests, most of the bandits have not been apprehended, and very little of the stolen oil has been recovered, which has greatly affected business. Since June of this year, maritime bandits have become even more rampant. The oil our company shipped to Chuan Kou (Chuan Port) was robbed in its entirety in the sea near Nanhui, Chuansha, Bailonggang, Jinshan, and other places. This included 1,500 pairs of barrel oil (note: 'pair' means tin) on the Xin Yonghe ship on June 21, 2,000 pairs of canned oil on the Dan Shunli ship on September 28, and 1,900 pairs of canned oil on the An Shun ship on October 3. Although we have requested that the relevant military and police agencies dispatch teams for strict investigation and arrest, months have passed without any recovery of the stolen goods. Such robberies are frequent, and arrests are neglected, causing commercial transport to lose its security. We are unable to even imagine what will happen to the future of our businesses. Therefore, we are requesting that you forward this matter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, which will then present it to the Executive Yuan of the National Government, ordering the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to direct the naval and land military and police along the coast to jointly conduct strict investigations and arrests, bring the perpetrators to justice, and recover the stolen goods to provide relief to transporters and alleviate merchant hardship." Based on this, maritime banditry is rampant today. If we do not strengthen suppression efforts, the future of commercial transport will be worrisome. Therefore, we have sent a letter to your association requesting that you urgently forward it to the National Government's Executive Yuan, ordering the coastal authorities of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to conduct strict investigations and arrests jointly, and also issue an order to the Navy Department to direct nearby warships to increase patrols to capture the stolen goods and suppress banditry. This is the situation. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, winter, bowing.

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce further states that maritime banditry has become increasingly rampant in recent years, which is an undeniable fact. There are many cases of goods being robbed during transport, reported by member associations to the relevant authorities, but few cases of arrests and recovery of stolen goods, or of severe punishments. The kerosene industry, which transports oil to Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, has been robbed as many as seven or eight times in the past year or two, and has yet to have a case solved. The industry has suffered losses. The implications of this negligence are not small. If arrests continue to be neglected and not thoroughly pursued, carriers will hesitate, which will greatly affect commercial transport and local security. Therefore, we respectfully request that your esteemed court and government review this matter and order a strict search and arrest along the coast to bring the perpetrators to justice, eliminate banditry, and provide security for merchants and travelers.

Hope for Resolution of the China Electric Company Labor Strike Dashed; Arbitration Requested Yesterday

The Bureau of Social Affairs Has Submitted the Case File to the Municipal Government.

The labor dispute between the workers of the China Electric Company, who are demanding a raise, and the management, after the Bureau of Social Affairs convened a mediation committee that failed to reach an agreement and set a deadline for both parties to resolve the matter themselves outside of the process by the 30th of last month. There was still no result after the deadline. The Bureau of Social Affairs conducted an investigation with both parties yesterday and learned that the possibility of a resolution was dashed. At the same time, the labor and management parties were separately instructed to be notified and await arbitration.

Methods for Collecting Products for Commercial Inspection to Participate in the Chicago Exposition

Issued by the Ministry of Industry

Our country will participate in the 1933 Chicago Centennial Progress Memorial World's Fair. The Ministry of Industry previously ordered its affiliated agencies to follow the preparations of the exhibit. After receiving the order, the Shanghai Bureau of Commercial Inspection stated that collecting the results of commercial inspection and displaying them at the Chicago Exposition is a comprehensive external promotion of our country's government inspection administration. The preparation of the exhibits is of utmost importance. Therefore, a request was submitted to the Ministry to formulate general guidelines for the exhibits and order the inspection bureaus to follow them to ensure uniformity, precision, and excellence in the exhibits. Subsequently, instructions were received that the preparatory work could be assigned to the various bureaus, and the Ministry's approval requested after appropriate general guidelines were carefully drafted. The Bureau immediately complied with the order, prepared the general guidelines, and submitted them to the Ministry of Industry for review and revision. The guidelines were then issued to the various bureaus for compliance and submission by the deadline. The methods are transcribed below:

Methods for Collecting Products for Commercial Inspection to Participate in the Chicago Exposition. (1) The Ministry of Commerce will use charts and written descriptions to show the overall progress of the commercial inspection system. (2) Each bureau will use concise text to describe the history and progress of the bureau from the time it was established to the end of the 21st year of the Republic [1932]. (3) Each bureau will use charts to show the organizational system of the bureau. (4) Each bureau will use films to show the location of the bureau. (5) Each bureau will use films to show the equipment of the bureau, piece by piece. (6) Each bureau will use charts to show the development process of commodities inspected by the bureau. (7) Each bureau will use charts to show the distribution of work in each inspection office of the bureau. (8) Each bureau will use text to describe the inspection methods of the bureau. Each bureau will use charts to show the bureau's achievements over the years. Each bureau will use films to show the bureau's working conditions, following its procedures. (9) Each bureau's inspection results, if they are to be represented by physical objects, the number of items will be handled in accordance with Article 7 of the Rules for the Collection of Exhibits by the Preparatory Committee for Participation in the Chicago Exposition. The preparatory work will be assigned to each bureau as follows: (A) Fruits, furs, wool, down feathers, sesame oil, and hemp oil will be undertaken by the Tianjin Inspection Bureau. (B) Beans, tobacco leaves, frozen meat, animal fats, and bone/horn/tendon glue will be undertaken by the Biao Dao Inspection Bureau. (C) Palm and tung oil, cottonseed oil will be undertaken by the Hankou Inspection Bureau. (D) Cotton, tea, plant diseases and insect pests, leather, silk garments, meat products, egg products, peanut oil, camellia oil, and silk fabrics will be undertaken by the Shanghai Inspection Bureau. (E) Cinnamon and timber will be undertaken by the Guangdong Inspection Bureau. (10) In addition to the provisions of the preceding articles, each bureau's exhibits may also reflect other ancillary operations, such as farms and serum production, in accordance with the provisions of Article 9. (11) Charts will be standardized at 65 cm long and 50 cm wide, and photographs will be standardized at 27 cm long and 19 cm wide (enlargements may be made at the discretion of the exhibitor in special cases). The quantity of exhibits, whether charts or photographs, should be kept to a minimum. Clear written descriptions are especially important. (12) All exhibits must be submitted to the Ministry of Commerce for review and consolidation by January 10, 22nd year of the Republic (1933), and then forwarded to the Micro Products Department.

Ministry of Industry's National Industrial Survey

All of Jiangsu Province Completed

The Ministry of Industry, in order to promote the development of national industry, will conduct a nationwide general industrial survey, and has ordered the Bureau of International Trade to handle it. The director of the Bureau, He Bingxian, immediately proceeded with the survey, starting with Jiangsu province. It began on September 1st, and was divided into two major districts, Jiangnan (south of the river) and Jiangbei (north of the river). The survey of the 31 counties in the Jiangnan district was completed in October. The Jiangbei district had 30 counties, divided into four sub-districts. The first sub-district surveyor, Xiao Guochou, was responsible for counties such as Qidong, Nantong, Rugao, Dongtai, Taixing, and Taixian. The second sub-district surveyor, Zhao Jian, was responsible for counties such as Jiangdu, Gaoyou, Baoying, Huai'an, Huaiyin, and Siyang. The third sub-district surveyor, Ma Jibo, was responsible for eight counties such as Fengxian, Peixian, Pixian, Suqian, and Tongshan. The fourth sub-district surveyor, Lu Guoxiang, was responsible for several counties such as Yancheng, Lianshui, Donghai, and Ganyu. The survey director was Hou Houpei. Personnel from all locations have returned to Shanghai one after another in recent days. The survey of all 61 counties in Jiangsu province has now been completed. It is currently being compiled urgently. The industrial section is about to be printed. It is estimated that the Chinese version can be published within the year. It is reported that the survey contains quite rich materials. The important forms that were pre-determined were generally complete in each county. The survey period was uniform, and all of them refer to the most recent situation within three months. When the survey personnel arrived, various county governments, bureaus, and public and private institutions were able to provide assistance. Therefore, with the exception of a few places, there were no great difficulties in the process. At a time when this kind of material is lacking, it will be able to provide important reference for all sectors in the future. Currently, about 20 people are involved in the compilation work. The name of the book will be "Chinese Industrial Records, Jiangsu Province". The sample will be printed soon, and the bureau will start taking pre-orders.

The Prerequisite for Foreign Rice Taxation

Domestic Rice Must First Circulate Freely.

The issue of taxing foreign rice has been much discussed, but no concrete measures have been heard of. A reporter from the National News Agency visited the responsible official of the National Tariff Commission to inquire about the latest situation. According to them, in October, the Ministry of Finance convened a National Food Conference in Nanjing, with participants from relevant ministries and commissions of the central government and representatives from six provinces, including Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei. Key personnel also participated in the discussions. At the conference, a proposal was drafted for a foreign rice import tax rate. The government is currently giving the case careful consideration, regarding the issue of food as a matter of great importance. The interests of provinces with a surplus of rice are slightly different from those with a deficit. It is necessary to ensure that the rice from surplus provinces can be supplied continuously, so that provinces with deficits have no need to rely on foreign rice, and there is no fear of food difficulties. However, in order to enable provinces to use their surplus to make up for the deficit, it is first necessary to abolish the precedent of provinces prohibiting rice from leaving the province, and the rice tax donations of all provinces. In addition, issues such as inconvenient transportation and high freight rates must be improved. Only then can domestic rice circulate freely. At that time, taxing foreign rice would be beneficial and without harm.

Ferry Sinks

Over Ten People Fall into the Water

Only Seven Rescued, Six or Seven Missing

Texaco Tugboat Caused the Accident

Yesterday morning, a Texaco tugboat collided with a ferry in the Huangpu River, causing the drowning of many passengers. The results of the investigation are described below.

Circumstances of the Collision: The No. 1 tugboat of the Texaco Oil Company departed from the Customs Wharf yesterday morning at 6:00 AM with passengers bound for the company's wharf at Gaoqiao Shabenz. At approximately 6:10 AM, while sailing in the Yangshupu River near River Buoy No. 17, it encountered the Xin Yunfei tugboat coming from Pudong, which was towing a ferry headed for Puxi (west of the Huangpu River). At the time, the wind and waves were strong. The Xin Yunfei tugboat was traveling downstream, and the Texaco tugboat was sailing head-on. After the Xin Yunfei tugboat passed, the Texaco tugboat collided with the towed ferry. The ferry was breached and immediately began to sink.

Ferry Sinks: As the ferry was struck it went down in the water. All passengers on the ferry, traveling from Pudong to Shanghai, were workers. Over ten people were in the water as the ferry sunk. After this incident, the Texaco tugboat and the nearby Water Police Station rushed to rescue the victims. Various sampans also went to retrieve those who fell into the water.

Seven or Eight Rescued: The Water Police Station and the various sampans rescued the following men and women: Peng Guangui, 31 years old; Ding Guangyu, 44 years old; Shen Miaoling, Yu Zhaohou, 26 years old; Zhang Cashi, 25 years old, Zhou Changfu, 45 years old; and Zhang Zhushi, 49 years old, a total of seven people. As all of them sustained minor injuries, they were sent to Renji Hospital for bandaging and dressings, and then allowed to return home.

Many Drowned: According to the investigation, over ten passengers on the ferry towed by Xin Yunfei fell into the water. In addition to the seven rescued, six or seven were missing. The Water Police Station repeatedly tried to recover the bodies, but no bodies were found. Therefore, the exact number of dead could not be confirmed. After the accident, Xin Yunfei reported the incident to the Jianghai Customs River Authority, and the number of victims and missing persons is currently under detailed investigation. Negotiations are being prepared with the Texaco Company, as well as requesting compensation and condolences. The damaged ferry has sunk in the Huangpu River.

One of the Assassination Case Perpetrators, a 19-Year-Old Cook

Taken Back from the Municipal Public Security Bureau for Interrogation, Claiming He Was Falsely Accused of Being Denied a Loan

Xiao Liu, a native of Anhui, was shot and killed on the evening of July 22nd around 9 PM at the intersection of Yulin Road and Jixiang Lane while seeking relief from the heat. The Yulin Road police station, led by Chinese Detective Lu Gengsheng and Detective Xie Wanfang, successively arrested the perpetrators Sun Lianfu and Wang Zhongde, who was apprehended at the Songhu Garrison Headquarters. The First Special District Court has heard and detained the suspects. The Shanghai Daily has previously covered these events. Another perpetrator, Housheng (also known as Han Sen or "Little Old Man"), was working as a cook at the security office located at No. 48 Fenglin Road in the Chinese district. The police station previously sent detectives to arrest the suspect, but were denied, claiming they needed to notify Mayor Wu and others. The police station received a phone call from the Municipal Public Security Bureau the day before yesterday, instructing them to take custody. The police chief ordered Detective Lu to rush to the bureau and bring back the suspect Han. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The police station's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, recounted the previous events and stated that the defendant was identified by Sun Lianfu, who confessed that Wang Zhongde had provided them each with a handgun and 50 silver dollars to shoot and kill Xiao Liu. Presiding Judge Shen is hearing the case, and requested the court to question the suspect before rescheduling a joint interrogation. Han Sen, when questioned, testified that he was 19 years old, from Anhui, and acquainted with Sun Lianfu. He denied going with Sun Lianfu to kill Xiao Liu in Jixiang Lane. He claimed that Sun came to the security office afterwards to borrow ten silver dollars to flee, but was denied, causing resentment and leading to the false accusation. The police lawyer, Zhang, stated that the defendant had already confessed at the police station, and presented the confession for review. Judge Zhao Linyu ordered that the suspect be remanded in custody to be jointly interrogated with Sun Lianfu and the others.

Changes to the Pig Tax Collection Method in Jiangsu Province

Lou Fumin Comes to Shanghai to Seek Support Without Success

Lou Fumin, a resettlement official from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance responsible for collecting pig taxes in Tongzhou, Rugao, Jingjiang, and Taixing, came to Shanghai from Nantong yesterday. This was due to the strong opposition from the local industry associations against illegal taxation. He aimed to explain the current collection situation to the fresh pig industry in Shanghai and seek their understanding, but without success. It is reported that Lou has also changed the collection method, from the original setup of checkpoints along the river to a unified collection. Regardless of size, each pig is valued at twenty yuan, and a tax of two jiao is levied at a rate of one-tenth of one percent. This is roughly similar to the previously proposed but unimplemented special business tax regulations. According to the special tax regulations for livestock, large pigs were valued at seventeen yuan and small pigs at five yuan, with a tax rate of two-tenths of one percent. Large pigs would be taxed at three jiao four fen, and small pigs at one jiao. Now, the valuation has been increased, and the rate has been reduced. The annual revenue is estimated to be one hundred thousand yuan, based on 500,000 pigs, with a total valuation of ten million yuan. Furthermore, Lou indicated that the collection rate could be reduced to eight-tenths of one percent. However, representatives from the fresh pig industries of Tongzhou, Rugao, Jingjiang, and Taixing convened a meeting yesterday to discuss and firmly oppose it.

City Chamber of Commerce Asks for Cancellation of Anhui Province Rice Permit Tax

The City Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance yesterday, requesting the abolition of the Anhui Province rice permit tax. The original text reads: "To the esteemed Executive Yuan and Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, on the 2nd of this month, according to a telegram from the Anhui Association in Beijing, on the 26th of this month, major domestic newspapers are competing to publish an article about the President of the National Food Regulation Association, Song Dai, sending a telegram to the Yuan, stating that all of you care about the people's food and protect their livelihoods, and people at home and abroad are ecstatic. People in Anhui are deeply impressed. Regulating the people's food is most important to circulation, and the key lies in exempting taxes. The telegram speaks in detail, and this association will not repeat it. This year, the rice-producing provinces have mostly had bumper harvests. Merchants are already burdened by the tightening of finance, and farmers are burdened by the harsh taxation of rice. Blocking the way out and stopping progress, rice prices are falling daily, and people are increasingly panicked. Even if we try to save it, I am afraid that it will be too late. However, the Anhui Provincial Government, under the pretext of restoring disguised likin, has set up a food export administration, levying six jiao per dan of food and three jiao per dan of miscellaneous grains, plus a 5% surcharge, armed extortion, tax networks densely distributed throughout the north and south of the Yangtze River, ignoring the clear order issued by the National Government on April 3, 1920, and violating Chairman Chiang's telegram of December 19, 1919. Moreover, it fundamentally contradicts the righteous propositions of the gentlemen and the Food Regulation Association. If we do not fight for justice, the future of the people's food and the rural economy are unimaginable. In addition to submitting a separate report from this association to Chairman Chiang of the Executive Yuan, we earnestly request a clear order to the Anhui Provincial Government to abolish it immediately in order to emphasize the public order. We also hope to be given strong support for the realization of beneficial regulation. How can the evil likin, which harms merchants and the people, be revived in today's Republic of China? There is no shortage of enlightened people in Zhongshan and Shanghai who dare to speak out for justice. The situation is urgent, please do not ignore it, etc.' The message arrived at the meeting. Upon investigation, rice is one of the hundreds of goods. Having a tax on exports is equivalent to a disguised likin. The collection of six jiao per dan, according to this year's rice price in Anhui Province, has almost reached 10%, which is unprecedented in the era of likin harming merchants. Although there are many bandits in Anhui, what about Jiangxi Province? Since Jiangxi Province had a bumper harvest this year, the income of the fields increased, and the rice inspection tax has been abolished. Therefore, Anhui Province should follow the same rules, eliminate abuses, and abolish political corruption. Otherwise, foreign rice will enter in endless quantities without taxes, while the province's agricultural products will have a surplus and cannot be sold, leading to the bankruptcy of the rural areas and plunging the people into desperation. The banditry is spreading, and we are thinking of cleaning it up. Why add fuel to the fire and prolong the chaos? We urgently telegraphed and request the esteemed Yuan and Ministry to investigate and order Anhui Province to immediately stop the rice permit tax for the sake of public convenience. Shanghai City Association bows respectfully."

Man and Woman Injured in Fire Escape, Carelessness on North Henan Road

At approximately 3:50 AM yesterday, a fire broke out at Yichangyong Coal Shop, located at No. 412, North Henan Road, Haining Road, in the Public Concession. Smoke filled the air, and flames soared, eventually spreading to the neighboring Taicheng Rice Shop, Yongfeng Plywood Shop, Dingchang Gasoline Lamp Shop, Zhou Faxiang Copper and Tin Shop, and stopping at the Zhihua Factory. Because the factory building was a solid brick wall, it was not easy to catch fire. At the same time, firefighters had already begun to rescue, so it was preserved. Because it was late at night, residents were all sound asleep. Suddenly hearing the fire alarm, they were anxious to escape. A man and a woman were injured after jumping from the building and were taken to the hospital for treatment by ambulance. The fire was extinguished around 5:00 AM. It is estimated that four houses were burned down.

I believe this is already well understood by your general manager. Now, due to the rising cost of living, the prices of all goods have increased. Taking the tram as an example, the starting fare used to be only 3 copper coins, but now it has increased to 7 coins, more than double the previous amount. The prices of other food, clothing, housing, and daily necessities have all increased several times. Therefore, employees of agencies such as the post office, customs, and railways have already increased wages and housing allowances to adapt to the needs of life. According to a survey, the lowest salary rate for workers in the above-mentioned agencies is more than 30 yuan, and the housing allowance is not included. The starting salary for workers was previously only 18 yuan. Although the general manager recently considered the workers' difficult living conditions and increased wages by 2 yuan, the maximum amount is only about 30 yuan. In these times of expensive goods, this small amount is far from meeting the needs of life. Not only is it impossible to support a family, but even personal needs are not enough. After repeated consideration, we have no choice but to submit nine requests. We hope that the general manager will accept and implement them. After careful consideration, the workers believe that these requests are extremely reasonable and do not go beyond what is reasonable and do not affect the company's economy. In the future, workers will have no worries about their lives, and they can work with peace of mind and strive for the development of the business, in order to achieve the goal of labor and capital coexisting and prospering. This is not only the honor of the workers but also the benefit of the company's future. We ask for your understanding and acceptance and look forward to a reply. We sincerely address the managers of the Great Eastern, Great Northern, and Pacific Telegraph Companies. The company did not give a definite reply after receiving the workers' request. The union sent Zhao Yanling and others as representatives to contact the general manager, Peng Sheng, but were also firmly rejected. Therefore, the emotions of all the workers are bitter, and further requests will be made today."

Lawsuit for Separation of Concubine

The Concubine Also Wants to Separate, Only Asking for the Return of 2,000 Yuan of Private Savings

Wei Zhichang, a native of Shaoxing, 34 years old, owns Xie Feng Silk Shop at No. 2, Zhufu Lane, Shilu, British Concession, selling various domestically produced silk fabrics from Dexing, Shengdan, Shengya, and other three silk weaving factories. The business is very good, and he has accumulated a considerable fortune. He married Chen, also from the same town, and has a son and a daughter. The son, Baojin, is 18 years old this year, and the daughter, Cuijuan, is 14 years old. They live at No. 27, Hengqing Lane, French Concession. In 1928, Wei worked as an accountant at Dexingchang Silk Factory in Zhangjiabang, and had a relationship with Zhu Suzhen (27 years old this year), a silk weaving woman in the factory. Soon after, he took Zhu as a concubine. In December of that year, he rented a house at No. 54, Weicheng Lane, Xiejiao, and lived together. They have now moved to No. 17, Xujiahui Road. They had a daughter, who soon died. Recently, Wei fell in love with someone else and suddenly developed a liking for the new and a dislike for the old. He accused Zhu of being addicted to gambling and unbearable to live with. He hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit in the Civil Court of the Second Special District, requesting mediation to persuade them to separate from the relationship of husband and concubine. The petition stated that the petitioner met the opposing party in 1928 at

Yihongyuan Brothel in Yaoer Alley: Her name was Xiaosuqin. The fifth old man pitied her suffering in the fire pit and paid to redeem her from the register. However, she was untamed and addicted to gambling. She secretly pawned and squandered all the petitioner's property. When the petitioner was away from home, the opposing party, fearing discovery, threw herself into the river in an attempt to commit suicide. She was arrested and detained in the old patrol room. Later, a friend named Zhu redeemed her, and her father also came to plead and wrote a letter of repentance, stating that if she gambled again and did not repent, she would unconditionally terminate the relationship. However, it was not long before she relapsed.

Too Ashamed to Face People: She voluntarily requested her husband to terminate the relationship in accordance with the agreement. Recently, she regretted the agreement and often came to make trouble and deliberately extort money, which was unbearable. Therefore, the petitioner requested the court to approve and order the termination of the relationship of husband and concubine. The court accepted the case and, at 10:00 AM yesterday, Judge Li Shouyi opened the Civil Court No. 3 for mediation. The petitioner, Wei Zhichang, was represented by a lawyer to state the circumstances of the request for mediation and separation. The opposing party, Zhu Suzhen, arrived in court with her lawyer, Ma Zhongnan. According to Zhu, her husband, Wei Zhichang, is utterly unconscionable. He had married two women before and left them soon after. I am the third he has married. After we lived together, he treated me very cruelly. Now he has left me with no clothes or food, and I have no choice but to die. He had previously sued me in the local court to return his clothes, but because his reasons were insufficient, the judgment was rejected. Later, he abandoned me and did not care for me. I went to his shop to ask him for money, but he refused to pay me. Therefore, I borrowed money to live. Once, I found him eating opium at a salted meat shop in Eight Immortals Bridge.

There was a Woman: Leaning against him. When he saw me, he started hitting me, etc. Zhu's lawyer then said that the opposing party used to work in a silk weaving factory, and the petitioner was also an accountant in the factory at that time. They met and were seduced into adultery, and then she was taken as a concubine. Now, the petitioner's claim in the petition that Zhu was a prostitute in Yihongyuan is a complete fabrication and can be investigated. Moreover, the petitioner previously sued Zhu in the local court for the return of clothes, and the judgment has been rejected.

Intending to Abandon: The opposing party, etc., and submitted the court's judgment. The judge asked Zhu Suzhen if she was willing to separate from the relationship of husband and concubine. Zhu replied, "I have suffered very deeply and am willing to separate. However, I had 2,000 yuan of private savings, which he took away. If he returns the money to me now, I can separate, otherwise I cannot." At this point, the court determined that the mediation could not be established and ordered a separate lawsuit.

Awards Ceremony for Storytelling Competition

The Director of the Education Bureau, as Chairman, Delivers an Address of Encouragement and Awards Prizes Separately for First, Second, and Third Place

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau-sponsored storytelling competition concluded, and the awards ceremony was held yesterday (the 3rd) in the auditorium of the Municipal Public Education Hall. The meeting commenced at 9:00 AM, with the presence of Director Pan of the Education Bureau, storytellers, judges, and over two hundred guests from various sectors. Director Pan served as Chairman, with Lü Hai, Ding Shoutang, and Xing Liru as recorders. Director Pan first delivered an opening address, stating that social education is even more important than school education because everyone, regardless of gender or age, has the opportunity to receive social education at any time. In particular, the skills of the storytellers can guide the entire society, so they bear a great responsibility for social education. In the past, scholars were ashamed to associate with storytellers, which created an invisible divide. Therefore, the Bureau organized this storytelling competition to draw the attention of society to the storytellers. He put forward three points: First, one must understand one’s own responsibility; second, one must make a practical and beneficial contribution to society; and third, one must innovate and learn from the past, ensuring that the material adapts to the trends of the times. The explanation was detailed, and the audience understood it in their hearts. Then, Section Chief Chen reported on the overall situation of the competition. Subsequently, awards were presented separately. Individuals received medals, certificates, and mirror frames, while groups received mirror frames presented to the Guangyu and Yuyu societies. Then, judge Xu Shen Dai provided guidance, and guests such as Tong Xingbai, a member of the Municipal Party Committee, and Wang Houlu of the Post Office delivered speeches, encouraging the storytellers. During the awards ceremony, the storytellers cheered and applauded continuously. Finally, representatives from the Guangyu and Yuyu societies delivered speeches of thanks. The ceremony concluded at 12:00 noon, and a group photo was taken before dispersing. The following is a list of the participants' scores in this competition, arranged in order of surname strokes: (Super Grade Eleven People) Shen Jian'an, Zhang Futian, Guo Shaomei, Huang Zhaolin, Cheng Xiaofang, Zhao Xiaoqing, Zhao Jiaqiu, Liu Tianyun, Jiang Ruting, Han Shiliang, Wei Yuqing, (Grade A Twenty-Nine People), Wang Zailiang, Wang Siquan, Tian Yiliang, Zhu Jiesheng, Zhu Yaoxiang, Zhu Yaoliang, Wang Yunfeng, Li Bokang, Wu Jun'an, Yu Xiaoxia, Zhou Xiaochun, Zhou Yuquan, Xia Hesheng, Xu Yunzhi, Jiang Fengsheng, Tang Fengchun, Tang Fengqi, Lu Fengxiang, Lu Xiao Xiang, Xu Jixiang, Zhang Yunting, Tang Kangbo, Feng Zimei, Ye Shengxiang, Yang Renlin, Zhao Hesun, Zou Senzhang, Zhong Xiaonong, Wei Hanying, (Grade B Nine People), Zhu Boxiong, Li Hanzhang, Lin Shaozhang, Hu Jinfan, Ling Youxiang, Tang Zhuping, Lu Fengyi, Huang Hefeng, Zhang Yuhua, (Two Additional People) Wang Lansheng, Li Xietang.

Obituary of Police Officer Yao Shaoqiu, Who Died in the Line of Duty

Mayor Wu and Others Send Wreaths and Funeral Couplets

Yao Shaoqiu, a petitioning police officer from the Qiuxinchang Police Station, District One, Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau, left work at around 7:00 PM on the 1st of this month. While passing near Zhangjia Alley outside Xiaonanmen, he was shot in the left chest by a bandit while attempting to apprehend the bandit. He fell to the ground, and the police station chief had him transported to Shanghai Hospital, but because of the serious injury, he died shortly afterward. After an investigation by personnel from the Shanghai District Court the day before yesterday, the coffin was sealed that evening. Yesterday afternoon at around 1:00 PM, the funeral was held. Mayor Wu Tiecheng, various organizations and groups, and various businesses in Nanshi all sent wreaths and funeral couplets, numbering no less than several hundred. The coffin departed from Shanghai Hospital, passed through Limalu to Shiliupu, turned into Dongmen Road, reached Zhonghua Road, continued south, and was temporarily placed at the Jianghuai Fellow Association outside Dananmen before being transported back to his hometown for burial. At the time, Municipal Police Bureau Director Wen Hongen, the Inspector General, the military band, police detachments from the first and second districts, and the various sub-stations, as well as the Bao'an Tuan (Security Corps), all went to hold the ropes of the hearse. It is reported that Officer Yao was twenty-three years old, a native of Yancheng in Jiangbei. He had served at the Qiuxinchang Police Station for over a year and was known for his diligence and conscientiousness in his work, earning him praise from his superiors. This time, he was tragically killed by bandits, leaving behind a widow and young children, and the situation is extremely desolate. Therefore, in addition to providing generous compensation, Director Wen has decided to prosecute the captured criminals to the fullest extent of the law in court.

Butterfly Trademark Still Pending Judgment

Huanan Society Requests Re-Examination

Huanan Chemical Industry Society previously submitted the portrait of Ms. Butterfly as a trademark and was approved by the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry. Subsequently, Family Industry Society claimed that it imitated its Invincible brand and Butterfly Chinese and Western characters trademarks and filed an objection. The Trademark Bureau ruled to revoke the Butterfly trademark. Details were recorded in yesterday's newspaper. Subsequently, Huanan Chemical Industry Society stated that the Butterfly trademark with the portrait of Ms. Butterfly had no possibility of confusion with the Invincible brand trademark and that the Butterfly Chinese and Western characters were submitted for approval after the society's approval. It cannot be used to oppose it. Therefore, it disagreed with the Trademark Bureau's ruling and requested that another committee be appointed to review it fairly according to legal procedures. The petition was several thousand words long, detailing the situation and providing sufficient reasons. It is still difficult to predict who will be right and wrong in the future.

Correspondence School

Excellent Results in Calligraphy Correspondence Course

Mr. Lü Gongwang from Beiping believes that calligraphy is an art and should be developed. Because rubbings from stone tablets are extremely complicated and difficult to obtain, he used 30 years of painstaking research on the foundation of brush holding, using extremely simple learning methods to practice fixed finger, wrist, and palm movements, and then shape and meaning, and founded a correspondence course with the aim of verification. There were more than 300 students in two sessions. Now the results of the first session have been published in this newspaper every month. If it can be popularized, it will truly solve the difficulty of writing. However, it is said that Mr. Lü is old and weak, and after the final expansion, it will be closed.

National Electric Industry Association Runs Correspondence School

The Education Committee of the National Private Electric Industry Association is now establishing a correspondence department in its planned electric industry school to train practical talents and serve the industry. It is divided into practical electrical engineering, electrical business, and electrical accounting courses. Domestic experts are invited to be editors. Classes will begin in January of next year and will last one year. The total tuition fee for all subjects, including the application fee, is 20 yuan. Graduates with excellent grades will be introduced by the National Electric Industry Association to major electrical companies for employment. Those with poor family circumstances can pay in installments as appropriate. The level is suitable for junior high school graduates or those with equivalent qualifications. Both men and women are accepted. Applicants can go to the Shanghai Correspondence Office of the National Electric Industry Association on the second floor of Central Road, Jiujiang Road, to obtain application forms and regulations.

National Humiliation Wall Chart Special Price

During this period of national crisis, it is truly a powerful tool to awaken the people and jointly resist the enemy. In order to promote it, the company is offering free sample sheets. Carnation Milk Powder Guessing Picture Contest

Anyone who buys a can of Carnation Milk Powder will be given a blank reply card by the store, listing eight colors and eight parts. Contestants can guess which color should match which part of the picture and submit it to the mailbox No. 860 in Shanghai, along with the store invoice. The standard picture has already been personally determined by the manager of Jishi Foreign Company for color matching, solemnly sealed, and handed over to Dong Xiangguang, Wen Wanqing, and Gu Yuqi for safekeeping. Those who are exactly the same as the original or the closest to it will be awarded prizes. The first prize is 300 yuan, the second prize is 100 yuan, and the third prize is 50 yuan, all issued in Shanghai Commercial Savings Bank vouchers, which is no different from cash. The following twelve winners will each receive a 5-pound can of Carnation Milk Powder. The competition period is from the 1st of this month to the end of the 1st of next year. The results will be announced in the Shen and Xin newspapers on March 1 of next year. It is reported that the number of submissions has been extremely enthusiastic recently.

Mr. Ye Dakang's Letter December 3, 21st Year.

Regarding the two questions raised by Ms. Zhang Yunqiu yesterday: (1) Why do countless couples fall from the boiling point of love to zero degrees? And (2) What methods can be used to remedy such a tragedy? I think it is very worthwhile to discuss because this phenomenon is really too common.

This question is certainly not one that can be answered by one person, but since your newspaper has submitted this question for everyone to discuss, I can also contribute my experience and opinions here.

Regarding the first question, I think this is a natural trend, just like the spring inside a clock. After being wound tightly, it will naturally loosen after running for twenty-four hours, which is not surprising. According to this theory, the way to remedy it is naturally only to "wind it up a few more times." How to wind it? Based on my experience, if a couple often has short separations, it can especially increase their love. As the saying goes: "New marriage is not as good as a long separation." Why is new marriage not as good as a long separation? This is the reason for not letting the spring loosen in one breath. So I think that the way to remedy it is to often have short separations, which is also a method.

Mr. Wu Jianqiu's Letter December 3, 21st Year.

I feel that everyone should participate in the discussion on the two questions raised by Ms. Zhang Yunqiu yesterday.

My opinion is: (1) It is very common for countless couples to fall from the boiling point of love to zero degrees. Couples who are already married or even have children cannot naturally be as intense as in the days of first love. If a young couple is "good brother" and "good sister" all day long, inseparable, twisted into a pile like a wedding candy, what would it be? However, it would be too terrible to go from the boiling point to the freezing point. As for the method of remedy, I remember that Mr. Zhang Boling once said: "If a wife can often change into a new dress, it can also increase the love between husband and wife." Although Mr. Zhang's remark was just a casual joke, I think it also makes sense. I will pass on Mr. Zhang's opinion for everyone to refer to and try!

Reporter's Note: The two questions raised by Ms. Zhang are indeed very worthy of discussion. The letters from the above two gentlemen, Ye and Wu, are only an "opinion" and not a "conclusion." I hope that all the good men and women in the world will actively express their opinions. This is not for others, but for yourselves.

Mr. Liu Jue's Letter December 3, 21st Year

The recent case in which the Anhui Fellow Association accused the disaster relief committee of Cha Mianzhong and others is very worthy of attention, but as of now, it does not seem to have caused any reaction in society.

Regarding this matter, I now have three questions, and I would like to ask your newspaper to take the trouble to give me a public reply:

(1) What exactly is this case about? What is the inside story?

(2) If the investigation is not factual, then those who are enthusiastic about public welfare will stop. How should those who make false accusations be punished?

(3) If the investigation is all factual, then how should Cha Mianzhong and others be punished?

Reporter's Note: Regarding the two questions (2) and (3), please everyone participate in the discussion.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Shandong coast is cloudy with northerly winds. The coast here and the East China Sea have uncertain weather with fog or drizzle and gentle cyclones, caused by low pressure passing through Jiangxi and moving northeast-east. The Yangtze River basin is cloudy with fog and winds are directionless. The typhoon in the Pacific Ocean was at 6:00 AM this morning, reaching within 120 miles of the intersection of 8 degrees north latitude and 138 degrees east longitude, moving westward. The wind force is unknown. In addition, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this city was 64.6 degrees at the highest and 50.9 degrees at the lowest. On the same day last year, it was 50.2 degrees at the highest and 47.7 degrees at the lowest.

Reader's Consultation Guidelines

1. Scope of Questions

(1) Politics and Economy (2) Law (3) Profession (4) Marriage (5) Family (6) Education (7) Rural Areas (8) Natural Sciences (9) Medicine (10) Social Issues

2. Method of Submission

(1) Please clearly state your name, gender, age, profession (or the school and grade), native place, and mailing address. (Detailed information is still required when continuing correspondence.)

(2) Present the issues you wish to discuss, using clear and detailed language to ensure the meaning is easily understood.

(3) Please write "Shen Bao Reader Consultation Department Received" on the envelope and attach sufficient return postage.

(4) The special stamp for the Reader Consultation column of this newspaper must be cut out and pasted on the upper left corner of the letter. Letters without the stamp will not be answered.

3. Handling of Received Letters

(1) We respect the reader's wishes. If the letter states a desire not to have the reply published in the newspaper, or a desire not to disclose their name when replying, we will comply.

(2) If the letter does not state how to reply, but this newspaper believes that a reply to one person has value for public reference, it will be disclosed in the newspaper.

(3) If the letter states a desire to have the reply published in the newspaper, but is limited by space, only the main points can be disclosed. If it is not possible to disclose it; or if the problem requires detailed research, it may be necessary to delay the reply and disclosure, which we hope the reader will forgive. However, if a reply cannot be published in the newspaper, a letter will still be sent.

National Central University Establishes Scholarship

Luo Jialun Discusses the Significance and Hopes for its Establishment Nanjing, 3rd dispatch: The National Central University has announced provisional scholarship regulations. President Luo Jialun spoke with reporters about the significance of establishing the scholarship and his hopes as follows: At this time of financial difficulty, the establishment of a large number of scholarships by National Central University demonstrates the greatest determination to promote scholarship and provide relief to students. When I was at Tsinghua University, there was also a scholarship system, which was specifically designed to provide relief to poor and studious students, but it is not easy to investigate the actual situation of students' poverty. If there are mistakes, it will cause more difficulties. Therefore, it is better to have open competition so that poor scholars can seek financial compensation based on their academic performance under the open competition system. Even if non-poor scholars win the scholarship, it is still an academic honor. Viewed from the perspective of promoting the arts, there is nothing wrong with it. After repeated long-term discussions at the university affairs meeting, it was concluded that all disciplines should be equally encouraged, so the department is used as the unit. However, the number of scholarships is seventy per semester and one hundred and forty per academic year. There are currently only 1,360 formal students at National Central University, which means that more than 10% of the students can receive scholarships each academic year, which is a huge number. I only hope that students will work hard to study and pay attention to their studies in the future. For examinations, jointly establish a spirit of absolute integrity, and professors should carefully assess performance and strive for fairness. Only then can the spirit of this initiative be fully realized. This scholarship focuses on rewarding students' daily studies because it is the foundation for all future in-depth research. The categories for the study of specialized problems are very numerous, and this university cannot take care of them all at once. I hope that people from all walks of life who have a special interest in a certain problem and want to promote it, such as foreigners, will donate special scholarships to the university at any time.

Ministry of Education Promulgates Kindergarten and Elementary School Curriculum Standards (13)

Arithmetic 1. Objectives

(1) To increase children's common sense and experience about numbers in their lives.

(2) To cultivate children's calculation ability to solve daily life problems.

(3) To cultivate children's habit of calculating quickly and accurately.

2. Types of Assignments

(1) Mental arithmetic, including in written arithmetic and abacus arithmetic, is the foundation of arithmetic. Mental arithmetic should be used purely as homework in the first school year, and the other school years should also emphasize both written arithmetic and abacus arithmetic. At least five minutes of mental arithmetic practice should be done during each arithmetic lesson. (2) Written arithmetic is taught sequentially in each grade. (3) Abacus arithmetic is taught from the fourth grade. It should be linked to written arithmetic and cross-referenced.

Arithmetic

Weekly Time for the First and Second Grades

1. Knowledge of size and length.

2. Knowledge of weight and thickness.

3. Recognition and application of the numbers 1 to 9.

4. Recognition of days, weeks, months, and years.

5. Calculation of daily attendance.

6. Recognition of the numbers 10 to 19.

7. Recognition and application of chi and cun (Chinese units of length).

8. Recognition of copper coins and silver dollars.

9. Recognition of triangles, circles, and squares.

10. Practice of various arithmetic games (such as patting a ball, throwing sandbags, etc.).

11. Basic practice of addition with sums not exceeding 9.

12. Basic practice of subtraction with numbers within 9.

13. Practice of addition and subtraction formulas involving 0.

14. Practice of addition without carrying within 20.

15. Practice of subtraction without borrowing within 20.

16. Practice of multiplication with products within 18.

Zhou Fohai, Director of the Jiangsu Department of Education

Inspection of Northern Jiangsu by Zhou Fohai (1)

Arrived in Nantong on the afternoon of the 1st and immediately inspected Provincial Nantong Middle School

Still needs to inspect Nantong for three days, scheduled to go to Rugao on the 5th

(Special correspondent from Nantong for this newspaper) Zhou Fohai, Director of the Jiangsu Department of Education, has spared no effort to rectify and enrich education throughout the province since taking office. Recently, he decided to personally inspect various counties to examine the general education situation and promote it. On November 30, he left Zhenjiang with Chen Xifang, head of the second section of the department, Xiang Jutan, head of the third section, inspector Cao Shutian, chief editor Yi Junzuo, and staff member Li Zhihong to go to Shanghai and then to Nantong. He arrived at 2 pm on the 1st of this month. Those who welcomed him included Zhang Dong, Nantong County Magistrate, Guan Jingcheng, Director of the Education Bureau, Qi Yunzhong, Director of the Construction Bureau, Li Disheng, Director of the Finance Bureau, Chen Yizhong, Director of the Public Security Bureau, Li Yongzhen, Head of the Agricultural Department of Nantong College, Qu Litan, Head of the Medical Department, Zhang Wenquan, Head of the Textile Engineering Department, Wang Shi'ai, Principal of Provincial Nantong Middle School, and Yi Zuolin, Inspector of the Department. They took six cars and drove straight into the city, staying on the second floor of the Nantong Club Hotel. After a short rest, they went to Provincial Nantong Middle School for inspection. Director Zhou inquired about everything in detail, and then Principal Wang led them to inspect the entire school's school buildings, equipment, layout, general courses, military training, art courses for normal school, etc. He also gathered the heads of various departments of the school and instructors for talks. He inquired and guided on the key points of combining teaching and training, improving standards, and political training. He was extremely detailed and earnestly urged them to pay attention to students' manners and discipline, promote the inherent national spirit of "respecting teachers and valuing the Way," implement the living of military training, and select exciting and impassioned music to enable young students to have a spirit of vigor in the strict life of discipline. After the conversation, it was already 6 o'clock, and they went to inspect the dining hall. In the evening, they went to the self-study room one by one to inspect the students' learning situation and experience in each subject, and gave instructions on reading methods until about 9 o'clock before returning to their residence. It is said that they are scheduled to inspect local educational institutions in Nantong from the 2nd to the 4th, and go to Rugao around the 5th.

Local News

The First Training Class for School Health Personnel Will Open Soon

In the three districts of Shanghai South, Zhabei, and Gaoqiao

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued instructions yesterday to municipal, already registered and private primary and secondary schools in Liunan, Zhabei, and Maqiao, stating that health education is the central plan for this year, and all the matters stipulated in the plan should be implemented in order. School health has a great impact on the health of young people and children. After consultation with the Health Bureau, the first training class for school health personnel will be opened in the three districts of Hounan, Zhabei and Gaoqiao starting on the 9th of this month to provide teachers and staff of various schools with knowledge of school health and proficiency in school health skills in order to fully implement the health subjects prescribed by the curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry. In addition to issuing the regulations for the above-mentioned training class with this order, you are hereby ordered to comply with and handle it accordingly. This order is accompanied by the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau Education Bureau's Regulations for the First Training Class for School Health Personnel: (1) The purpose of this training class is to train school health and administrative personnel and promote the implementation of health courses. (2) All personnel from municipal primary and secondary schools in the three districts of Hounan, Zhabei and Gaoqiao listed below should attend the lectures, except for special circumstances that have been reported to the Ministry of Education in advance for approval: 1. The principal (attached note: director) or administrative director; 2. The moral education director; 3. Physical education or health course teachers. (3) Each registered private primary and secondary school may send one person to attend the lectures. (4) The training class will have one director and one deputy director, who will be appointed by the Health Bureau and the Education Bureau after consultation. (5) The training class will have several lecturers, who will be jointly hired by the Health Bureau and the Education Bureau to be specialized personnel. (6) The duration is from December 9 of this year to January 17, 22nd year of the Republic of China. (7) Before the lecture, each school should fill in the names, genders, and positions of the attendees (hereinafter referred to as students) and report them to the Education Bureau separately. (8) The school hours for Hounan and Zhabei districts are every evening from 7 pm to 9 pm except for Sundays. The teaching hours for Gaoqiao district are every Monday morning from 9 am to 12 pm and afternoon from 1 pm to 4 pm. (9) The training class locations are: the municipal Xicheng Elementary School in Hounan district, the municipal He'an Elementary School in Zhabei district, and the municipal Gaoqiao Elementary School in Gaoqiao district. (10) If a student is absent, the school to which he/she belongs should first report to the Education Bureau and obtain permission for leave. (11) The academic performance of the students will be assessed by the lecturers, and the Education Bureau may send personnel to investigate at any time. (12) Students who complete the course and pass the examination will be given a certificate by the Health Bureau and the Education Bureau jointly, but those who are absent for more than one-quarter of the total course time will not be given a certificate.

Authorities in the British Concession Prohibit Broadcasting and Lectures

The Joint Association of Private Schools in the French Concession Decides on Measures

Will Visit Mayor Wu Tomorrow to Request Protest

At the Same Time, Go to the Municipal Education Bureau to Inquire About the Results

The Joint Association of Private Primary and Secondary Schools in the French Concession of this city originally planned to start broadcasting and lecturing at the Zhongxi Pharmacy on Four Horses Road on the 5th of this month to publicize the development of Chinese education in the concession by the French Public Bureau and to arouse the common attention of citizens. Later, the authorities in the British Concession sent detectives to prohibit it, so it could not be held as planned tomorrow. The association is dissatisfied with the handling of the British Concession authorities. Yesterday, the standing education committee Ma Jiazhen drafted a plan and obtained the consent of all the executive and supervisory committee members. It was decided that tomorrow morning, all the committee members will go to the Municipal Government to visit Mayor Wu to request a protest to the Public Concession authorities to vent public debt and protect the freedom of Chinese people in the concession. In addition, the association previously summoned various committees by the Municipal Education Bureau to talk about the request for subsidies, which has been contacted by the Municipal Education Bureau and the Municipal Government to the French consul for progress and promised to reply within a week. Now that a week has passed, it is decided that all executive and supervisory committee members will go to the Municipal Education Bureau tomorrow at the same time to inquire about the results.

Ten Thousand Bamboo Moral Education Achievements Are Excellent 丨 Group B Competition This Afternoon

The National National Language Education Promotion Association held a National Language Art Competition at Wan Zhu Elementary School in Shanghai.
