Opening Ceremony The opening ceremony was held at 1:50 pm. After the salute, the judges first reported the competition rules, and then Cao Peizi, representative of the Shanghai Municipal Party Department Executive Committee, gave a speech. The competition started at 2 pm. Competition Rules 1. The competition this year is limited to one-act plays. 2. This competition is divided into two groups, A and B. Grades 3 and 4 of elementary school are Group A, and Grades 1 and 2 of senior elementary school are Group B. 3. The order of the competition is based on the lottery number. 4. The performance time of each script should not exceed 5 minutes. The timer will ring the bell once after 4 minutes, and ring the bell again after 5 minutes, and stop immediately. 5. This competition focuses on speaking and expression, not on makeup and scenery. 6. When performing, tables and chairs should be used. The same association prepares the stage layout, which is free for the contestants to arrange. After the performance, the contestants should remove them. The rest of the props are also managed by the contestants themselves. 7. The judges are divided into three categories and six items: (1) The meaning of the play, ideology 10 points, structure 10 points, a total of 20 points, (2) Speaking, pronunciation 25 points, intonation 25 points, a total of 50 points, (3) Expression, expression 15 points, action 15 points, a total of 30 points, which are recorded separately by the judges, and the total score is ranked. 8. The results of the judging will be announced the next day. 9. The award will be given on January 1, 22nd year of the Republic of China, 10

High School Students Still Did Not Attend Classes Yesterday Demanding Unconditional Return of Expelled Students

Why Talk About Irreversibility Han Talks About Students Obeying Orders to Attend Classes to Avoid Prosecution

Jinan, 3rd dispatch: He Siyuan said that expelled high school students must submit a letter of repentance and obey the examination before being allowed to return to school. Those who instigated the unrest must be identified and planned to be persuaded to attend classes again on Monday.

High school students still did not attend classes today. The teachers and staff of the department gathered the students to persuade them to attend classes. The students demanded: 1. The expelled third-year students must return to school unconditionally. 2. First and second-year students are guaranteed not to suffer any sacrifice, that is, to attend classes. However, third-year students must be identified and submit a letter of repentance before they can return to school. The Education Department is handling the matter according to the provincial order, and it is feared that it will be difficult to withdraw the order.

The Provincial Government ordered the Education Department: In order to issue instructions, I recently received a winter telegram from the Executive Yuan, stating that according to the Ministry of Education, He Siyuan, Director of the Shandong Education Department, repeatedly telegraphed that thousands of secondary school students in Jinan gathered to petition the provincial government and the provincial party department and issued a declaration opposing the graduation examination. The situation is serious. In addition to telegraphing the director of the department to earnestly implement the examination and not be lenient, the Shandong Provincial Government should be ordered to strictly prohibit and punish the students who took the lead in order to rectify the school spirit, etc., arrived at the Yuan. It has been found that the middle school graduation examination is an order issued by the Ministry of Education to all provinces. How can some students in the province wantonly oppose it? The department should immediately be ordered by the provincial government to strictly prohibit it, punish the leading students, and rectify the school spirit, etc. In addition to replying by telegram, the department should be ordered to earnestly comply with and report back for investigation and not violate this order.

Han talked about the fact that the academy ordered strict handling of the student unrest, but if the students obeyed the order to go to work, they could not be prosecuted.

Rain or Shine This Morning, the International Walking Race, Six Nations Vie for the Championship

The Chinese Team Prepares to Maintain its Champion Title

Among the Six Nations, Britain is the Strongest Opponent

Seventeen Miles and One Hundred Yards Completed Inside the Racecourse

The International Walking Race this year will be participated in by six countries including China, Britain, France, Ireland, Russia, and Italy. Regardless of the weather, it will commence at 8 AM sharp this morning at the intersection of Carter Road and Jing'an Temple Road, racing the long distance of seventeen miles and one hundred yards, following the same route as previous years, ending in front of the grandstand at the racecourse.

丨Chinese Team Athletes丨

(1) Shi Jinsheng　(2) Zhou Quanyu　(3) Xie Xingdao　(4) Ge Jinwen

丨New Record Special Award丨

Mr. Cheng Yize is enthusiastically sponsoring this walking race. In addition to awarding a badge and certificate to those who complete the entire course within the stipulated time, Mr. Cheng will also provide a special award to anyone who can break the record of two hours, twenty-seven minutes, and three seconds. Mr. Cheng firmly believes that Shanghai's race walkers will create a world-shattering record. Therefore, the referees and race walkers must pay special attention.

丨Radio Broadcast丨

Marconi Wireless Telegraph Company, in conjunction with the Wireless Radio Department of the police and XCBL, will be broadcasting the race. Therefore, those at the grandstand of the racecourse will be able to know the progress of the race along the route.

丨Introduction of New Rules丨

The introducers must pay attention to the new rules. There shall be no introducers from the starting point to Breen Avenue. From there, each race walker may have one introducer, and at the eight-mile mark, they may change to another introducer.

丨Attention for Cars丨

Those in cars and motorcycles, please pay attention to yielding to the race walkers. It is hoped that motorcycles will not follow the race walkers.

丨First Place Time丨

The first place should arrive at the racecourse before 10:32 AM. Before the awards ceremony, a speech will be given by Chairman Fang Deng, and Mrs. Hu Erfu will present the awards.

丨Chinese Walking Association Meeting丨

The Chinese Walking Association held a joint meeting of racers, introducers, and referees at its headquarters today. Attendees included Shi Youhui, Zhou Yuyu, Yu Zichen, He Borong, and more than forty others. The meeting began at 2 PM, chaired by Shi Youhui and recorded by Lu Yutian. The chairman first reported that foreigners are greatly ashamed because our China has won the championship for four consecutive years, so they have come up with various methods in this session to contain and restrict us, reducing our strength, such as limiting the participation of Chinese people, firstly, prohibiting the wearing of rubber shoes without heels, secondly, and not allowing introducers to crowd together, preventing the latter from advancing, thirdly. In short, foreigners intend to take our championship by this means. It was also rumored that Mr. Zhou Yuyu was about to withdraw. Now, Zhou was persuaded by Yu and Lu Yutian, Fu Zichen, and Zhang Zaocun Shi Jinsheng and others to consider the overall situation, still able to attend with illness, to vent anger for our China and maintain the championship. Even if physical strength is not added and is slightly late, people can also forgive it, and so on. Then discussed as follows, if the introducer cannot attend due to business, please determine another one as soon as possible to facilitate the race at that time, and change immediately, five or six people. Furthermore, the responsibility of the introducer is very important, and it is related to the excellent performance of the racer. Therefore, when introducing, in addition to taking care along the way, the time must be reported every mile so that the racer can be clear and can speed up or slow down the pace to rest. At the small turning point, it is necessary to take care of the racer to cross the road diagonally, but it is not allowed to use the turning point to run and jump over to prevent being punished. When the racers are tired, it is necessary to drink and sing the pace one two one two, or left and right and so on, continue to sing down to show encouragement. In this conference, the referees, in addition to wearing green ribbons, also have red white base "Judge" words, have the power to punish racers, all our Chinese team members, pay attention to it, and introducers must report to the racers at any time, when surpassing other racers, regardless of Chinese or foreign, it is never allowed to look back, even if it is not conceited, the loser will eventually feel despised. Next, distribute referee ribbons, armbands, special issues, and passes. This year, the Chinese Jockey Club also generously agreed to borrow, and I hope that our Chinese team members and staff will gather upstairs at 7:15 this morning (in order to contact everything, and change clothes, etc., to each mile point, handled by Mr. Aegis, but this time, because the Boy Scouts happened to be in charge of aviation propaganda, it was not possible to fulfill the wish, so I changed to invite seventeen students from Arabaidstulu Shanghai Elementary School to stand with flags to facilitate the competition of the racers.

Stout Cup Two-Week Competition

Jinan Eliminates Donghua

One to Zero, the situation is extremely intense and the actions are rough and terrible.

Open and secret arrows retaliate for grievances, which is by no means a good situation.

丨West Police Force and French Business School Tie Five to Five丨

丨Agaer Eliminates Elementary Level with Ten to Zero丨

Luo Haiguang's header breaks through the Donghua goal, resulting in Jinan defeating Donghua with a score of one to zero.

In the Stout Cup, Donghua was eliminated.

Jinan people in the second week of the competition, yesterday after the rain cleared up, there were few spectators on the baseball field. The overall situation of this battle almost fell into a confrontation of public anger and private revenge, with the possibility of triggering force. Many spectators also scolded the Jinan players for their unworthiness of Donghua players, which was despicable and vulgar, and self-degrading. It is a pity, it is a pity. As for the rough actions of the Jinan players, it was the main reason for arousing public anger. However, Donghua should not be allowed to be arrogant. Both sides have considerable blame. However, one is an open gun and the other is a secret sword. It is not a good situation to fight each other. However, the guidance of the fire line started from the injury of the secret arrow. The two sides already had a rift at the dinner party of Mayor Wu the night before. The reason is that the reporter is really inconvenient to repeat more to avoid further inciting trouble. It is hoped that both sides will donate their prejudices and return to their old friendship, and strive for technical competition to win glory for my China.

The Overall Situation is Grim

Yesterday, the field was muddy and inconvenient for Yi to run and compete, so the situation was equal, each relying on luck.

Ten minutes into the start, Jinan scored through Luo Haiguang's header from Liu Zukan's cross, becoming the focus of resolving the victory or defeat.

After that, Jinan had many shots on goal, either high or wide, but none of them were on target. Even if there were, they were saved by Zhou Xianyan.

Once, Chen Zhenhe shot hard, Zhou caught the ball and fell to the ground. Chen Zhenxiang, Mei Hongbao rushed up and kicked Zhou Xianyan's body indiscriminately, the situation was dangerous, and the referee ordered a free kick.

Zhou Xianyan argued with Chen Zhenxiang, and Zhuang Shihong joined the vortex. The two sides had the intention of using force. Chen Zhenhe, Jiang Shanjing, and the referee tried their best to mediate before it stopped. However, the situation after that was almost completely in a rough state of fierce rushing and tripping, and the game was thus reduced in color.

In the second half, Donghua had two chances, one was Chen Hongguang's fierce shot, the ball went into the arms of Jinan goalkeeper Xie Quanhe, and the other was Li Yichen's dribbling into the unmanned area, Xie Quanhe failed to save and fell to the ground, and Li also fell to the ground at the same time, the ball rolled forward and went out of bounds along the goalpost.

These two goals not being scored were Jinan's great fortune, but Xie Quanhe's special care yesterday, and strict precautions are also the reason why Jinan was not defeated.

The Situation in the First Half

At three o'clock, the war clouds were densely covered. Jinan took the lead and kicked off several times, but there was no tense situation. Although there were charges and battles, both sides had no achievements.

Ten minutes later, Liu Zukan, Jinan's left winger, shot a ball to the front of the Donghua goal, and center Luo Haiguang stepped forward and headed it in, which was the first great achievement.

Donghua's loss of the ball was not due to Zhou Xianyan's failure to save it, but to the accident of Zha Xun'an's fall.

Since then, the two sides have still been in a chaotic situation. Although Donghua had two corner kicks, Li Yichen and others tried their best to attack the goal, but they were helpless and only shouted in vain.

Then saw Jinan Chen Zhenhe and Luo Haiguang approach and attack the goal, Zhenhe shot hard and the ball was caught by Zhou Xianyan, but the ground was slippery and he fell to the ground holding the ball, Chen Zhenxiang and Mei Hong冲上去踼之, the situation was very dangerous, the referee blew the whistle to relieve the danger and penalized Jinan a free kick, from then on, each side held prejudices and acted wilfully, and the ball battle fell into a bad situation.

Jinan shot several times without success, Donghua advanced into the Central Plains, Xie Quanhe blocked Li Yichen's shot, Chen Yutian ambushed by the door, took advantage of his sharp hand to kick the ball into the goal, the audience clapped their hands and celebrated the success, but it was offside and the judgment was invalidated, which was the situation in the first half.

The Situation in the Second Half

After the break, the whistle sounded again, and the ball was moved, and the ball entered Jinan's hands, Chen Zhenhe ran hard and dribbled near the goal, fearing that he would lose his success in one fell swoop, and kicked in a hurry, before he could use his strength, it was steadily saved by Zhou Tie.

Donghua's formation gradually became scattered after that, and at this point, Jinan was repeatedly warned by the referee for improper actions, so the two sides became more and more deteriorated, pushing and shoving fouls, each saw it, the audience's voice was also very bad.

After Chen Yutian of Donghua failed to attack the goal once, he dribbled the ball and quickly passed it to the Jinan goal, Hongguang shot quickly, but unfortunately, he happened to enter the goalkeeper's arms again, and the success was defeated at the last moment. After a period of mixed battles, Qian Jingyi passed a ball to the front of the Jinan goal, Xie goalkeeper fell to the ground, and Li Yichen took the opportunity to dribble the ball forward, but he also lost his footing and fell, the situation was so tense, the ball rolled slowly forward, and it was seen that it must be hit, but it hit 余裏去了, the audience could not help but stamp their feet and sigh.

Seeing that the twilight was deep and the time was about to end, the entire army of Qiu Hua rushed into the enemy camp and fought against the city with one heart and one mind. Jinan also retreated to defend the whole army, hoping to maintain the final situation. In the melee, Jinan finally won with a score of one to zero, and Donghua suffered the tragic situation of the first failure.

Free Talk

Short Story

Wedding Night (3)

— Bing Xin

In fact, this is not a big deal. What struck Miss Xiu the most was when her mother gave birth to her youngest sister. It took a day and two nights, but the child still didn't come out. She personally saw from the crack in the door the various situations of her mother rolling around in pain, shouting loudly, and crying with tears streaming down her face. She just felt chills down her spine. What made her especially scared was hearing that this time the child came down with feet first and head last. This was really too dangerous. Anyone who heard it would stick out their tongue. Not to mention Miss Xiu. Her fear and aversion to childbirth were simply indescribable. From then on, she made up her mind never to marry and dreamed of her single life day and night.

It was really too strange. No one could have imagined that in just half a year, she would marry an old husband who was forty-eight years old, short in stature, with yellowish-black skin, countless wrinkles, and a face that looked completely like a monkey. Others naturally couldn't understand Miss Xiu's pain and only felt that "a fresh flower was stuck in cow dung" (Note 3), which was a bit of a pity. However, her parents felt nothing but glory and happiness and were simply completely satisfied. This was naturally because the son-in-law was an only son, and the family property was well-off. In addition, the son-in-law was diligent and thrifty and could earn money. It was said that he might even become a rich man in the future. This was equivalent to the daughter's property, which would be used for her whole life in the future. The responsibility of being a parent was to marry off their daughter. Being able to marry a daughter to a son-in-law with family property was, in their eyes, a model of a benevolent father. Although the son-in-law was thirty-two years older than the daughter, the matchmaker's face was too great to refuse, and what did it matter? A man should be older than a woman.

"Although Xiu'er's marriage is good, I just think that man is a little too old and unmatched," Miss Xiu's mother said with emotion one day.

"What's unmatched? It's good that he's a little older so he can take care of her. As the saying goes, 'Marrying an old man is like getting a treasure, marrying a young man is like getting a weed' (Note 4). Moreover, even if he becomes rich in the future, you don't have to worry about him marrying a concubine. Don't you think so?"

"Amitabha, you're thinking so far ahead, just"

"Two years older is nothing to worry about, thirty-two years older is really too much. Do you think she can live her current life?"

After all, she was a kind mother, and she actually started to cry.

"Don't be ridiculous, what's there to cry about? It's not like sending her to the tiger's mouth. Even if he's forty-eight, fifty-eight, or sixty-eight, what does it matter? Don't you know that Old Master Fu in Wangjia Chong is seventy-five years old and still wants to marry a fourteen-year-old girl as a concubine? Isn't that girl still human!"

Miss Xiu's father was originally a kind person, but for some reason, he had been arguing with his wife lately about his daughter's marriage. Every time he said a few words, he would get angry. Today was the same. Not only was his attitude bad, but his tone was also particularly sharp, probably because he had just had some wine.

"That's not right, it's immoral!"

After a long pause, Miss Xiu's mother said this timidly as if in protest.

"What's immoral? It's not like killing her and cooking her for wine."

"Humph! It's more terrifying than killing her!"

"Look, when Xiu'er marries over there in the future, as long as they consummate the marriage, I guarantee you won't have any problems."

"Humph! You wait and see!"

Anger

Laugh for a while, cry for a while, unrestrained, unconcerned, carefree, count me as comfortable. But looking at the present, thinking about the past, suddenly a whim, and deeply feel that crying and laughing are not right, then immediately stop laughing and stop crying, stirring up a ten-thousand-zhang nameless fire of anger.

Anger, how ugly! Face full of red, eyebrows vertical eyes horizontal, rubbing fists and wiping palms, fierce, like a living demon king out of the world, naturally there is no modesty so elegant and gentle, so peaceful and good-looking.

But humility must also have a limit. If in your home, you know that someone is coming to rob today, and someone is coming to rape tomorrow, making it uneasy to eat and uneasy to sleep, you also elegantly and gently, peacefully and good-looking, make a bow, bow, and even kowtow three times, "Good heroes, little student is being polite here," is there any reason in the world? I can't!

Even our ancestors, although they have always lived in the land of etiquette, were not without "anger". Look: "Angry hair rising up to the crown," what a majestic look! "Shouting to cut off the Ba River," what a scary thing! As for "One anger and the princes fear," "One anger and peace the people of the world," that is even more deeply related to the safety of the world and can be regarded as a model of anger. Therefore, even if we occasionally get a little angry, although it is inevitable that it is a little ugly, it does not hurt the overall situation, and it will never become an unfilial descendant.

However, anger must also be appropriate, and it should not be unreasonable, and it should not be hard-mouthed and empty-hearted. When Zhang Laoer brothers don't agree with each other, they immediately get red eyes and fight, which is called unreasonable trouble; Wang Danian was robbed, scared to hide in the quilt and dare not breathe, and after the robber left, she cried and scolded the murderous thieves at the gate, which is called hard-mouthed and empty-hearted.

However, there are too many Zhang Laoer and Wang Dalian of our noble country in front of us, alas and sigh, "One anger and peace the people of the world," if this anger does not come out, what will the country do?

Kingdom of Children

— Wu

"England is the kingdom of children," Yukio Tsurumi of Japan once said this.

Really, all of England's social life is centered on children. If we go to a bookstore in London, then we can find piles of children's books displayed there. Fairy tales are also mostly from England, it can be said that except for Andersen alone, many fairy tales come from England.

Ordinary Londoners are very fond of children. In terms of preserving the human race, they have a very high respect for the personality of children. Even in poor families, there will be a children's room. This room is a sacred area, and children become true sovereigns. Of course, that is the kingdom of children. Adults entering this kingdom must be very respectful and solemn.

Most families in London have a small garden, and it is also not uncommon to have piano or lawn tennis court facilities. Also, because London is always smoky, which hinders the physical development of children, many people want to move to the suburbs, so that children can get as close as possible to nature. This is of course a reflection of the psychology of caring for children.

English children's mothers, in order to make their children the successors of the English nation, do not spare their efforts to train their children in the wind, frost, cold and heat, hoping that they will erect the flag of the British Empire on the ice island of Antarctica. Therefore, there is often a kind of respect between mother and child, but perhaps it is also a kind of estrangement: the result is the formation of an opposition between two personalities.

The Current Status of German Women

— Jian

Speaking of German women, one cannot help but be amazed. They possess the courageous spirit and the perseverance of French women, yet they are more reserved than their French counterparts. They finally gained suffrage after the war, but it was not easily obtained; they struggled greatly. Like the women's movement in any country, the primary goal is to improve the status of women and create new environments for them, and the German women's movement is no exception.

In 1908, as a result of the women's movement, German universities were opened, and women were free to attend lectures, unlike before, when they were restricted. At the same time, as long as a woman had skills, she could occupy a higher position in any industry. This can be said to be the first stage of the German women's movement. However, the rapid change in the status of German women occurred during the European War. At that time, men, young and old, went to the front lines to fight. All that remained were women. What kind of work were they good at? What kind of work were they interested in? In this emergency, they had no room for consideration, so they bravely took the place of all men, even in manufacturing military supplies, driving cars, and other extremely heavy work. They were able to operate freely, just like men. From then on, not only did they break the long-standing habit of underestimating women, but they also created a glorious page in the history of the women's world. This is the second stage of the German women's movement.

When the European War ended, a group of veterans returned from the front lines, hoping that women would return to their families and give up their positions. However, they had experienced the taste of work, achieved considerable success, and felt the interest in it. They were unwilling to simply remain at home. In particular, women from the intellectual and leisure classes were even more unwilling to spend their days in the same boring life as before, so their desire for work became even more intense. In addition, as a result of the fifty-two-month war, the people of Germany were plunged into bankruptcy, and a group of widows and orphans had no choice but to seek employment to maintain their survival. At the same time, more than half of the men died for their country on the battlefield, resulting in women outnumbering men by nearly three million, which led to difficulties in women finding marriage partners. Since women could not find spouses, they had to make a living, so many female soldiers were added to the workforce. According to the facts, German women are not only able to take on all kinds of tasks, but also able to jointly shoulder the responsibility of national economic revival with men. They also have considerable ability in administrative aspects. By this time, everyone had gradually recognized the possibility of women's participation in politics. However, most people still held a lukewarm attitude, and thought that women's duties were only to handle household affairs, and there was no need for them to participate in politics. Therefore, the women's suffrage movement became even more heated. As a result, the German Parliament finally passed a resolution in 1918 to grant women the right to vote, and the following year, the German Constitution clearly included the provision that women have the right to vote and to be elected. This is a rough overview of the changes in the status of German women after the European War.

Street Scene in Early Winter

— Xingzi

The cold wind has driven away the autumn, which still carried a hint of warmth, and brought a deeper coldness. At this time, early winter, which makes the poor panic, has arrived! The streets of early winter are particularly lively all day long, but on the other hand, they are also particularly desolate. Laughter is mixed with crying, champagne glasses are soaked with blood and tears, which is precisely the foundation of modern cities, and also precisely the symphony that is indispensable in modern cities.

Let's take Nanjing Road as an example:

The sound of drums and music jingles on both sides, and large banners flutter in the middle of the road. And when night falls, the red and green electric lights make people's eyes dazzled and their minds flutter. This is the seasonal hawking of early winter. The glass windows of large department stores are full of fox legs, mink furs, warm and delicate Parisian wools... This is the seasonal winter clothing. Every company and store opens its bloody mouth, and the "heroes" constantly squeeze, chase, and roll in and out. Everyone has a pair of greedy eyes and a ferocious mask, ready to seize the flesh and blood of others and pretend to be happy themselves.

Cars constantly shuttle back and forth, carrying the "heroes" returning in triumph, so the streets are often filled with yellow dust, showing a particularly lively scene.

But, if the time is in the middle of the night, the streets change into a different world.

The street is like a dead snake, sleeping silently. The faint streetlights shine on the snake's back, and the cold wind blows from the darkness, weaving into a net of death. At this time, the hawking girls, like ghosts, tremble under the cold lamplight. And in the dark corners, the weak curl up, like dogs, with the whips of hunger and cold lashing their bodies mercilessly. Subdued sobs and mournful moans turn the streets into a living hell.

Winter has come, and the poor are panicking, but isn't the end of winter spring? The arrival of spring is probably not far away!

Long Novel

The Crossroads of Era and Love, Part Four

— Zhang Ziping

While thinking, he tore open his sister's letter to read. He learned that his brother-in-law's job had been handed over two weeks ago. Haiquan's brother-in-law, Liu Weiying, through the introduction of his old classmates and the use of some bribes, had served as the director of the ×× Tax Bureau in Guangzhou for more than a year. When Haiquan was still in Guangzhou, he had heard people say that this ×× Tax Bureau was a very good position, but it could not be occupied for long. Now it seems that their prediction has been realized. His sister's letter also said that his brother-in-law didn't want to stay in the south anymore, and might come to Nanjing after the New Year to look for a job. Then, at that time, they might live in Shanghai, and they could see each other often. After reading his sister's letter, he slowly tore open Liu Peizhu's letter to read. He learned that his brother-in-law had been dismissed on suspicion of embezzling public funds. The content of her letter was written like this.

"Mr. Haiquan,!! You have written to me several times, not allowing me to address you as such, but I still address you this way. Although I am willing to do what you ask of me, at present, I simply don't have the courage!! It's not that I have forgotten the previous agreement!! I also feel very embarrassed to open my mouth to you, and even more embarrassed to write it down. I hope you won't be as suspicious as you were in Guangzhou, and constantly promote your theory of exclusive love. Our friendship only seeks mutual sincerity, and doesn't need those formal expressions, right?

"Have you met Sister Zhen in Shanghai? She is a formalist, and has the life and attitude of a thorough bourgeois. I hope you won't mention anything about us in front of her. Because she will definitely oppose our union. As for the reason, it's not just because she is an extreme reactionary against free love, but also because she is extremely sensitive about our!! especially your, material life, and harbors a kind of disdain. In short, love is supreme, beyond everything. However, sometimes it is helpless, and we have to be dominated by the environment,!! especially by the economy. Of course, I am not advocating that the economy will dominate our love. I only hope that Haiquan will pay attention to this point, and work harder to break the unfree environment of our love.

"If we can't open up this free path, a free path that is sufficient to promote the progress of our love, then even if we hastily unite, in the future, in life, we will still be extremely struggling and extremely painful, right?

"On my sister's side, no matter what, you should go there once a month to perfunctorily deal with them. Even if you don't like their character, and don't want to see their life. But in human society, it is impossible to seek things and people that completely fit one's own ideals, right? Because I know your aloof and cynical temperament, I dare to give you this piece of advice. If you sincerely get closer to them, then you will definitely be able to move them. Then, you can also reduce the resistance to our future union. To be fair, Sister Zhen is just a bit arrogant. As for her heart, it is still extremely pure and kind, just like my mother. Unfortunately, her temper and attitude are similar to my father.

"My brother's ×× Director has been dismissed, fortunately without investigation. This is entirely due to the power of Commander Huang. What I told you before has come true. My brother is a petty corrupt official. He already has a lot of money, and is happy to step down. I heard that he will go to Nanjing next spring to look for a ××× Director. I regret that I can't graduate for a while, otherwise I would immediately go to Shanghai with them to discuss the issue of schooling with you.!! I might drop this boring women's normal school in Guangzhou and immediately come to Shanghai to discuss the issue of schooling with you."

Cotton Mills Handling Light Business

The raw cotton business remains sluggish. Various mills report that the yarn market is unlikely to improve, so they are purchasing less raw cotton. The sources are estimated to be 199 bales of Yao cotton and 860 bales of Tong cotton.

Foreign Cotton Falls More Than Rises

Yesterday, American cotton was weak due to political news favoring short positions, Southern hedging, and a lack of buyers. Futures fell 9 to 16 points, and spot prices fell 15 points. British cotton futures fell 1 to 3 points, and spot prices rose 3 points. Egyptian cotton spot prices fell 3 points. Indian cotton was firm due to buying by brokers and speculators. American Cotton Affected by Gold Pound, Lost Its Stability in the Past Week

A New York telegram on the 2nd reported on the cotton market during the week. The war debt issue has not been reversed, and the gold pound has depreciated, causing the cotton market to lose its stability in the past week. The first notice quantity for December was 40,000 bales, all of which were taken by important spot traders. It is said that 10,000 bales will be shipped to Europe. The decline in the cotton market is not only due to the above reasons, but also directly related to the liquidation of large long positions. However, Southern hedging is very small. Recent private estimates are sufficient to strengthen the current public impression that the next government report will exceed 12 million bales. The textile market is unusually slack, so buyers are concerned that demand is limited and are generally waiting for developments.

Grain and Flour Market Weakens

丨Foreign Wheat and American Wheat Both Fall Back丨

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, various months turned to a declining trend. The quotations for foreign wheat and American wheat fell by 2, 3, 4, and 6 jiao, respectively. The extreme highs of the previous day were inevitably impulsive at this point. Therefore, after the opening prices, the market in various months was sluggish, losing slightly more than one fen compared to the previous day's closing price. The market remained unstable in subsequent sessions. When the afternoon session opened, sentiment remained poor, falling nearly one fen compared to the morning. However, after the second session, it gradually strengthened again. Currently, there are still inquiries about the sales of spot flour. The factories have very thin inventories, and the rising gold market has somewhat affected the continued ordering of foreign wheat. Therefore, sentiment is improving, and progress is steady. However, the continued ordering of foreign flour in Tianjin will strike a blow to flour sales at the beginning of the year. As a result, the current month fell by 5 li compared to the previous day, January fell by 1 fen 2.5 li, February fell by 1 fen 5 li, March and April fell by 1 fen, and May fell by 7.5 li.

Wheat Futures Sellers Dominate

Yesterday, after the wheat futures market opened in the morning and afternoon, the market in various months generally turned to a declining trend. As foreign wheat had fallen back by 2, 3, 4, and 6 jiao, the bullish atmosphere of the previous day inevitably weakened. Because traders had sold off when prices rose sharply the previous day, their holdings were slightly larger. Trading was more subdued yesterday, but sellers dominated, and prices fell at the opening. Future movements should be watched based on foreign wheat. As a result, January fell slightly by 1 fen, March fell by 4 fen, and April fell by 5 fen. There are no comparisons for the rest.

Chicago Wheat Weakens

A report from Xinfeng Foreign Firm (2nd day): Chicago wheat fell by 1.125 to 1.75 cents due to profit-taking by bulls and the weak New York stock market. Daily trading volume totaled 40 million bushels. The market prices on the 2nd are listed below:

Southern Dried Goods and Lily Buds Show Slight Price Increases

Recently, activity in the lily bud market has increased slightly. The opening price for spot goods has risen by several qian. Top-grade vegetables are priced at 14 liang, followed by 12 liang 7 qian to 12 liang. Transactions totaled about 200 packages. The prices in Zhenjiang are 11 liang 7 qian to 5 qian for the upper and middle grades. However, current inventories in Shanghai and Zhenjiang are still high, so they have not yet experienced price increases. Nevertheless, market prices are indeed low, so there should not be a large drop in the future market. Yesterday's market price for top-grade vegetables was sold for 14 liang 2 qian, followed by 13 liang to 12 liang 5 qian. Xuzhou vegetables were 11 liang 2 qian, and old inferior vegetables were 7 liang.

Metal Pure Antimony Reaches New High Price

Since pure antimony fell back, the market has plummeted. In the past two months, due to the impact of military affairs (bandit suppression) in the producing area (Hunan), arrivals have sharply decreased, causing the Shanghai standard to soar. The highest price reached 250 liang per ton. At present, the export business seems to be developing, so sentiment is even stronger. The standard has reached a new high price and is estimated to be 260 liang per ton. It is said that more than 20 tons were offered yesterday.

Northern Merchants Actively Purchase British Steel Plates

丨Spot Goods Are Extremely Scarce丨

British steel plates have been actively sought after by merchants from Tianjin, Qingdao, Yantai, and Hankou. Due to the scarcity of spot goods, prices are rising. For example, 2.5 li is estimated at 8 liang 2 qian 5 fen, 5 li at 6 liang 5 qian, 7.5 li at 6 liang 2 qian 5 fen, 1 fen at 6 liang 1 qian 5 fen, and thick colored steel at 6 liang.

Investigation of the Shanghai Cost of Living Index for November of the 21st Year

The National Tariff Commission recently published the Shanghai Cost of Living Index, stating that the index for November of the 21st year compiled by the commission was 108.7, which is 4.2% lower than the previous month and 13.2% lower than the same month last year. Except for February of this year, when the index showed a high peak due to the Songhu battle, the index has fallen back to around 120 since April. The decline has been particularly significant in the past two months, and this month it has fallen below 110, the lowest record since August of the 18th year. Since the Shanghai Wholesale Price Index compiled by the commission has repeatedly fallen over the years, it is natural that retail prices will also decline accordingly. In terms of major categories, compared to the previous month, food fell by 7.4%, clothing fell by 6.1%, and fuel fell by 4.4%, all of which experienced sharp declines. In terms of individual items, white sugar, green vegetables, and cotton have all suffered severe declines. Other items such as rice, soybeans, coarse cloth, fine cloth, cotton drill, firewood, and coal briquettes have also depreciated, which is the main reason for the decline in the overall index. The index of each category is compared in the table below.

Shenbao Local Supplement

Brief Comments

Blood Head

— Fo

In Shanghai's lower and middle classes, the term "blood head" can often be heard. To explain it, it generally means "empty shell," "pretending to be foreign," putting on airs, or having a good appearance. Without "blood head," one cannot become a fashionable person. Without "blood head," one cannot start a new business. Without "blood head," there is no Shanghai society. Therefore, Shanghai society can be called a "blood head" society.

If a woman doesn't wear a coat and her long dress underneath doesn't show by a foot or so, she's not "blood." If a student's long gown doesn't reveal a section of Western-style trousers, he's not "blood." If you sit in a rickshaw and the front isn't covered with felt, if your hat isn't worn at a rakish angle, if you don't have an Old Gold or Green Tree brand cigarette in your mouth, you're not "blood." What are the signs plastered all over shops saying "sacrificing capital for a big sale"? It's "blood head." What is it when you hire a few cheerleaders upstairs to play "wedding" music? It's also "blood head." There are so many examples of "blood head," it's almost everywhere you look. This is called a "blood head" society.

Opening an exhibition and not inviting a few important Party and government officials as figureheads doesn't count as "blood head." If those few important people don't travel by plane, and aren't touring the mountains in the east and playing in the water in the west, that's also not "blood head." If you don't have airplanes and cannons running rampant everywhere, you can't be called a top-tier "blood head" powerful nation. In the tense state of an international conference, if you don't loudly proclaim withdrawal from the League of Nations and put on an act, that's not "blood head." Therefore, the use of "blood head" is very broad, and its effects are numerous. This is called a "blood head" world. Therefore, when I think of the term "blood head," I think of many "blood head" undertakings. I won't give any more examples now. In short, if a person isn't "blood," they're a wooden dummy and can't stand in society. If a store isn't "blood," it deserves to die and can't exist in the market. If a country isn't "blood," it's out of luck and can't establish itself in the world. "Blood," alas, "blood"! It's truly "blood"! If you meet a few friends who eat from the trough of ideology, they're bound to shout "Long live 'blood head'!" But when I turn my head and think, why be "blood"? What is "blood" good for? I can't answer that question. I need to ask a few "elders."

Literary Arts

Two Quatrains Inspired by Hearing of the National Government's Return to the Capital

— Wang Fuding

Don't say the royal aura of Jinling has faded away; fixing the tripod in a peaceful place has precedents from past dynasties.

Looking back at arrivals and departures, my heart is greatly grieved; waves beat against the solitary city amidst the night's desolation.

Fortunately, the general disregards his own safety; he reverses the sinking of half the country's rivers and mountains.

On the road to Luoyang, Yuanquan advised the emperor to return; he re-entered Jinmen, wiping away the dust in celebration.

Literary Work

A Letter

— He Wenxin

He climbed onto the counter to sleep, tears falling naturally onto the pillow. Past events, like a series of movies, played out in his mind:

"How happy I was at school! There were thirty or forty classmates my age. After class, we gathered together to do physical exercises and play hide-and-seek… Everyone was happily laughing like little birds in spring!"

"When I returned home, my mother picked me up, gave me a kiss, and then ran to the kitchen to cook. She was afraid of being late and missing school. She left all the good food for me to eat, willingly enduring hunger herself. No one in the world loved me more deeply than she did! Really, making me an apprentice wasn't her intention. The night before I left her, she said with tears in her eyes, 'Fu, I'm sorry, as your mother! It's not that I don't want you to advance like other children. I also know that being an apprentice is a dead-end job. But middle school costs two or three hundred dollars a year, and university costs five or six hundred dollars a year. Your father could work himself to death and still not earn that much. Rather than failing halfway through, it's better to have a trade of your own, so you can at least earn a living in the future.'"

"From then on, I was taken by a black-awning boat to this place far from home! That is, I fell from a warm stove into an icy snow cave…"

He compared the past and the present, and the more he did, the more unbearable this life became. He got up as if determined to do something. His two small cheeks were flushed with excitement!

From his close-fitting shirt, he pulled out two pieces of paper, an envelope, and a pencil. He gathered all the characters he had learned at the national elementary school, and by the moonlight seeping through the cracks in the shop door, he resolved to write a letter to his mother.

"Mom! Today the boss beat me again, and my colleagues are also bullying me. They are not as lovable as my mom and my classmates. I want to go home, but I don't know the way. Mom! It would be best if you came to take me back!

Your son, Fu"

After he finished writing, he read it aloud and felt very good about it. Then he wrote on the envelope:

"Please give this to my mother."

He folded the letter, put it in the envelope, and felt much calmer. He planned to secretly put it in the mailbox tomorrow when he went to buy cigarettes. He slept very well that night and had many sweet dreams.

(Inspired by reading Anton P. Chekhov's "Vanka." November 28th)

Continued New Interpretation of Hidden Language

— Yun Zong

That slippery customer, Lytton, in his "League of Nations Investigating Committee Report," on the settlement of the Manchurian question, does not respect our country's sovereignty in any way, and is almost promoting international co-governance, really is the northern barbarians talking about everyday matters (a bunch of nonsense)!

In this eve of capitalist collapse, the number of unemployed people in various countries is increasing day by day. The unemployed form groups, demonstrating today and petitioning tomorrow. The authorities have no satisfactory way to solve this problem. It is really like riding a horse on the bow of a boat (at a dead end)!

Han Liu Qixin in Shandong, uncles and nephews fighting in Sichuan, causing the people to be frightened and flee, hurrying like a homeless dog, panicking like fish escaping the net, sleeping in the open and eating in the wind, suffering from hunger and cold, truly like a mute eating coptis (an unspeakable bitterness)!

Liang Zuoyou boasted greatly, actually saying that he would donate 30 million to the government. The Executive Yuan initially treated him with the courtesy of a distinguished guest, but later the magic trick was exposed, and it was only then that everyone realized that he was greatly cheated! It is really like a sparrow eating chaff (empty joy)!

Nowadays, our country is suffering from internal and external troubles, which are coming one after another, but the whole country, up and down, is mostly living in a drunken dream. The revival of the Chinese nation, I am afraid, is like a monk marrying a wife (never going to happen)!

Women in Shanghai

— Yi Ping

"Women in Shanghai!" A writer in a certain magazine said with emotion:

Broad roads, maple trees, a corner of a red building, the harmony of violins and singing; a luxurious car, speeding, huge window decorations, high heels tapping on stone steps, expensive Parisian perfume, handbags, banknotes; cinemas, handsome companions, passionate kisses, the scent of flesh overflowing, children not admitted! Pleasure-seekers selling their souls, women in Shanghai!

But, friends, please show me that you have run out of the ivory tower, taken off your tinted glasses, and stood at the crossroads!

Before dawn, the factory sirens roared wildly. In every nearby shack, many ghosts crawled out from tattered quilts. Each haggard face leaned close to a mirror with a missing corner. They washed their faces with cold water, filled their stomachs with leftover cold rice, prepared enough food for lunch, and hurriedly ran to the factory, fearing that they would be scolded by the foreman for being late, or, even worse, have their wages deducted. The few cents they earn with sweat and blood every day. In the factory, for example, after the wooden spindles are weighed together with the yarn, their careful work ensures that the weight is not reduced when returned. They work tremblingly every day. When they are sick, no one cares! When they die, no one pities them.

And there are:

When the lights are on, Shanghai's sleepless night begins. There are people who absolutely cannot enjoy themselves and sell their bodies to provide pleasure for others. In Shanghai, these women who live in underground tunnels seem to have broken away from the category of "people," and are merely instruments for venting lust, for people to use. White powder and red rouge cover up their original faces, raise their tempting voices, and avoid the ears and eyes of the police, giving insincere smiles to those they seek to exploit. They are not lowly women; they can also enjoy themselves. But they cannot sell their entire souls, so they sell their bodies piecemeal.

The examples are enough. Women in Shanghai!

Broad roads, maple trees, a corner of a red building, the harmony of violins and singing; a luxurious car, speeding, huge window decorations, high heels tapping on stone steps, expensive Parisian perfume, handbags, yarn tickets; cinemas, handsome companions, passionate kisses, the scent of flesh overflowing, children not admitted! Women in Shanghai!

The Poison of Early Marriage

— Kang Shi

Auntie Liang was a widow, already over fifty years old. She only had one son, named Gengsheng, so she doted on him very much. At the age of fifteen, she got him an apprenticeship at a foreign goods store, and he was highly praised by his teachers and friends!

When Auntie Liang was observing widowhood, she was only in her forties. Now, seeing her son grown up, how happy and joyful her heart was. It was not in vain that she endured ten years of hardship observing her widowhood. Therefore, in her happiness, a tragedy was created, what is commonly called "extreme joy breeds sorrow"!

Because Chinese customs particularly value descendants, especially women, who like to hold their grandchildren and great-grandchildren around their knees, of course Auntie Liang had this mentality. Therefore, she asked relatives to be matchmakers and find a daughter-in-law, hoping to hold a grandson soon and continue the family line. Therefore, Gengsheng was married at the age of sixteen.

When Gengsheng got married, he was still an apprentice, without the ability to support himself. Moreover, he was at the age of development, and the fire of youth was so vigorous! He often returned home on false pretenses to enjoy his paradise of gentleness. On the side of his studies, he was more negligent than usual, fearing the reprimand of his teachers and friends. However, being in this environment, Gengsheng's behavior was no longer what it used to be. He often argued with his teachers and friends, and eventually he was fired. Of course, it is not easy for an apprentice who drops out of school halfway to find another job, so he stayed at home idle.

Since Gengsheng stayed at home idle, he did not think about making a living and relied on his mother for everything. Auntie Liang often ordered Gengsheng to find a job, but how could Gengsheng, who had no skills, do it? As the saying goes, "One who sits and eats will empty a mountain," so after half a year of Gengsheng's sitting and eating, the economy gradually became strained. Therefore, the mother blamed the son, and the wife blamed the husband, and the family had no peaceful day. Gengsheng, having suffered the cold irony and ridicule of his mother and wife, repeatedly became ill with anger. Moreover, Gengsheng had married early, fundamentally depleting his vitality. Water could not nourish fire, and Yin could not nourish Yang, so he was bedridden for three months and eventually passed away to the turbid world. Auntie Liang, who had sought to have descendants as soon as possible, cried so sadly! In her anger, she even blamed her daughter-in-law, saying that she was destined to be a "widow"!

Alas! The above family, because they wanted to have descendants as soon as possible, instead cut off their descendants. There are many such families in China. Therefore, the population of various countries is increasing day by day, while the population of our country is decreasing day by day. For the future of the nation, this is worthy of concern!

Fiction

Sympathizers (Continued - Part 3)

— Zhang Henshui

Meng Guobao cracked melon seeds, seemingly finding a kind of fragrant and crispy enjoyment in it, quietly chewing away. While everyone was silent, one could hear the rustling sound of Wang Lao'er's wife fanning herself. Under the silvery moonlight, although one couldn't see her appearance clearly, one could still make out her strong but not clumsy figure. She seemed to know that this gentleman from the city was glancing at her, sometimes touching her hair and sometimes tugging at her collar. Meng Guobao finally couldn't help but speak, saying, Lao'er, you've kept this threshing ground very clean! Wang Lao'er said, I share it with Zhao Xiaogouzi; I wouldn't need it all myself! Meng Guobao said, This place of yours is not bad. In this village, you don't have to mix with others. And it's only separated from the big threshing ground over there by a vegetable garden. You can hear people talking over there clearly from here, so it's not lonely. Wang Lao'er said, People who are used to living in the countryside aren't afraid of being cold and isolated. Mr. Meng, you're not used to living in the countryside, are you? The countryside isn't as fun as the city. Meng Guobao smiled and said, Do you like living in the city? Wang Lao'er, hearing this, couldn't help but be filled with envy for the city. Scratching his head, he said, Of course! I often tell her that if I become rich, I'll definitely take her to the provincial capital to see the big pagoda at Yingjiang Temple. Meng Guobao laughed, There are so many fun places in the provincial capital, not just that one pagoda! Now they've built roads along the riverbank. Wang Lao'er said, Really? I heard that roads are different from the streets in Peiping. They're paved with foreign cement and gravel. When it rains, there's no mud on the ground, and when the wind blows, there's no dust. They're as flat as a tabletop. At night, the electric lights along the road are so bright that you could pick up a needle that fell on the ground. Meng Guobao said, Isn't that so? Wang Lao'er's wife couldn't help but interject, asking, I heard that electric lights don't use oil, and no one has to light them. They turn on by themselves when it gets dark and turn off by themselves when it gets light. What's the reason for that? Isn't that a treasure? Meng Guobao wanted to laugh but, upon second thought, realized that laughing would offend her, so he tried his best to hold back. Wang Lao'er said, Do you know? It's a divine thing. The foreign teachers at their school said that the fire inside the electric light is the yin and yang fire collected from the Lightning Goddess. His wife said, Oh! That's incredible! Divine things can be used so casually. Meng Guobao felt that this was an opportunity to speak, so he said, Sister-in-law, how would you know? The ghost stories of the divine era have all become reality now. People used to say that immortals could fly through the sky on clouds and mist, but now we can fly through the sky on clouds and mist as long as we spend a few tens of dollars on an airplane. Wang Lao'er's wife hadn't yet replied when Wang Lao'er interjected, saying, Mr. Meng, why are you so polite, calling her Sister-in-law? Everyone in the village calls her Wang Ersao. You can just call her Wang Ersao. Meng Guobao laughed and said, Lao'er, I have to correct you on that. What's the difference between "Sister-in-law" and "Ersao"? Wang Lao'er said, Oh! I hadn't thought of that. It seems like "Wang Ersao" is her given name. Calling her "Sister-in-law" would be elevating her. Meng Guobao said, Calling her "Sister-in-law" is proper. You're several years older than me. Aren't we like brothers? Hearing this, Wang Lao'er felt genuinely happy from the bottom of his heart and stood up, exclaiming, "Oh!" Then, thinking that people might not see his friendly expression under the moonlight, he sat back down and slapped his thigh, saying, Mr. Meng is truly a good person! Whether Meng Guobao had heard his words or not was unknown because, at that moment, he was thinking that calling a sixteen-year-old bride "Sister-in-law" might make her uncomfortable. However, if this kind of woman hadn't married Wang Lao'er and was still a village girl at home, she would truly be a naturally beautiful wildflower. But it's a pity... As he thought this, he heard the chirping of crickets in the weeds under the bean trellis, and the evening breeze blowing from the water made the leaves and the tall grass on the ground rustle. Just then, a white cloud in the sky covered the moon, and a thin layer of shadow rose from the ground, making the threshing ground quiet down. (To be continued)

Amateur Weekly

The Mission of This Publication

After a short period of preparation, "Amateur" is now able to meet with readers as scheduled. We have already stated in our call for submissions: "The purpose of this publication is to supplement industrial and commercial education and improve amateur life." Readers can understand the nature and objectives of this publication from its name, so it may not be necessary to write this routine! mission! text.

However, in today's world where the life of the nation and the economy of society are in danger of perishing and collapsing at any time, how should we awaken the people of the country, and how should we establish a great organizational foundation to cope with the unprecedented transformation in world history that has already begun? How can we revitalize the national spirit that is fading day by day and save the precarious national destiny? The reporter cannot help but have a few humble opinions, which I sincerely offer to readers on the day of this inaugural issue as the ultimate goal of our joint efforts in the future.

We know that shop employees, workers, and apprentices are indeed the backbone of social organization. However, only a minority of these backbones have received a decent education. Looking back at the situation during the year of national crisis, most of them were wandering aimlessly, not knowing what to do. However, whether it is to transform the social environment or to save the nation from danger, it is necessary to have adequate preparation in terms of knowledge in order to shoulder the important task of "connecting the top and bottom". Therefore, the first mission of this publication is to improve the educational level of the backbone of society! shop employees, workers, and apprentices.

We also know that Shanghai is a prosperous place, but it can also be said to be a place of all evils. The singing, dancing, and extravagant life are most likely to erode the ambition of aspiring young people and numb the pure and flawless souls of young people. Therefore, we loudly call for the young people who are responsible for saving the country to not fall into the trap. Therefore, the second mission of this publication is to improve the amateur life of the industrial and commercial circles.

We recall this year's commemoration of "September 18th". The whole city was lifeless. Furthermore, the enthusiasm for resisting inferior goods is declining sharply. All of our employees must at least blame ourselves for not being united and not working hard enough. Therefore, the target of this publication is the entire society, not individuals. We hope that readers will raise research and discussion on various issues such as how to train ourselves, transform our environment, and revive the nation at any time. Therefore, the third mission of this publication is to unite the strength of the masses and jointly shoulder the heavy responsibility of saving the country.

"Amateur" is small, but the mission is great. We hope to work together to save the dying national destiny!

Problem Discussion

How to Treat People? Service Issues

— Pan Yangyao

In general, a person who serves in society deals with three things: things, matters, and people. "Things" are fixed. As long as you are meticulous and careful, and use scientific methods of analysis, you should not be afraid of solving them easily. "Matters" are more difficult because they can be simple, complex, and sometimes have various changes. However, if you can be calm, quick-witted, and use scientific management methods, and have the spirit of patience and hard work, you can also solve them easily. Only the problem of people is the most difficult to deal with and is not easy to please. No matter what level of employee you are, you always feel that dealing with people is the most difficult thing. I don't know how much grievance and how much idleness I have suffered in this process. Everyone has an unspeakable difficulty. Junior employees often feel that senior employees are putting on airs and acting important. Senior employees often feel that junior employees are stubborn, disobedient, and unwilling to work hard. As for colleagues, there are certainly many who are good, but there are not many who get along well. If you don't say that he is hiding laziness, he will say that you are taking shortcuts. If you are respectful to senior employees, you will be said to be flattering. If senior employees talk to him more, you will be said to be favored. It's not right to do this, and it's not right to do that. It's really difficult to be a person. In fact, according to me, as long as people get along in the right way, it is not difficult. Most things in the world are ordinary and can be solved. As long as you eradicate the biggest root cause, you will be happy everywhere. There are three words for the root cause of people getting along:

One is the word "doubt". Nine out of ten misunderstandings come from the word "doubt". One is the word "pride". Nine out of ten conflicts come from the word "pride".

One is the word "anger". Nine out of ten scoldings come from the word "anger".

A person's facial expression is the most difficult to control. Sometimes it is slightly rigid. In the eyes of a suspicious person, he will think that I have some opinions with him. In fact, he is suspicious and annoyed by himself. However, because of this, I have to pay more attention to the expressions on my face. Sometimes, when I am carried away with joy, I can't help but be a little arrogant, and people will think that I am arrogant to him. Sometimes, when I am unhappy, I speak louder and have a stern face, and people will think that I am getting angry. Conversely, putting yourself in their shoes, what about yourself? Yang Jiaoshan, a gentleman of the Ming Dynasty, said: "A person who is willing to think for others when things happen is the best." That's great. Think for others in everything in advance, and it will be easy to treat people. Yesterday, a friend of mine said: "I went to solicit advertisements for the credit agency directory. When I met the manager, he was willing to tell me a few words and sometimes asked me to sit down and give me detailed instructions. Unfortunately, when I met a staff member, he was frowning while working. I was not sensible and asked him a few questions. He either ignored me or said not to bother him, and rudely rejected me. It is really 'easier to see the King of Hell than a minor devil'." He also said: "Sometimes senior employees agree, but junior employees still make things difficult in every way, treating me as if it is very important. It is really 'Bodhisattvas lower their eyebrows and Vajras glare'." After he finished speaking, I said, "You have certainly suffered grievances, but you have not put yourself in other people's shoes. The manager is certainly busy, but there are always people to handle things for him. Each person has a specific responsibility. He is only in charge of commanding and leading, so he can still talk to you. Ordinary employees are writing, calculating, typing, and working very hard. When you go to ask him questions, he will certainly show an unhappy expression. If you speak from the perspective of forgiveness, it is also understandable, so don't get angry." The friend laughed when he heard me say that. Another friend told me: "I worked in a certain company. At first, my monthly salary was twenty yuan, and I was very satisfied. Three months later, the manager suddenly added ten yuan. People congratulated me, but who knew that my pain came from then on? My colleagues gossiped, saying that my salary was high or that I was good at flattering. In fact, I only know how to do my job. I would do it the same way whether I was given a raise or not. Since the raise, whenever there is a difficult task, they all say that this matter requires you. Everything is pushed on me. I am certainly not afraid of doing more things, but how can I bear it if it goes on like this?" After hearing this, I said, "Do you have a family?" He said no. I said, "How is your life?" He said, "I still feel that I have more than enough." I said, "Then, please ask for a pay cut yourself and see what they say." This friend listened to my words and did as I said, and now he is fine. "Less pay, more work" may also be the key to getting along with people. However, I also want to talk about being a senior employee or leader. When I was recuperating in Moganshan, my old friend Qin Hancai sent me a book called "Leadership Studies". At first, I was not willing to read it because I thought that Chinese people have a desire to be leaders. The problem with people is that they like to be leaders, so there is no need to talk about leadership studies anymore. Later, when I read it carefully, every sentence came from experience and every sentence made sense. It can be seen that it is really not easy to be a person above others. Because it is not easy to do, so you have to study it. I feel that the most pertinent words in the book are that the value of a leader lies in being able to "tolerate others", being able to "harmonize colleagues", being able to "guide employees", being able to "recognize talents", and being able to "take the strengths of others and make up for one's own weaknesses". I remember that Mr. Huang Renzhi once said to the leader of a certain factory: "You should calculate accurately and check thoroughly on matters and things, but you should not do so on people. You must be honest, generous, and tolerant. Then everyone will be happy to be used by me. This is the general attitude that is necessary for dealing with people in the world." If those who are in a position above others keep these golden words in mind, then people will be at ease and wholeheartedly be used by you. They will not complain even if they are tired or refuse even if they are bitter. The difficulty of dealing with people will not be a problem.

Life in the Business World

The "Four Heads" Life of an Office Worker

— Hui Zun

It seemed as if yesterday's fatigue had not fully recovered when the alarm clock on the bedside rang at 7:30. I was suddenly awakened from my dream by it, and I felt that the time of the night had passed too quickly. I was too lazy to get up, but driven by life, I had to break away from the warm blanket, and my body felt a little cold.

After getting up, I went through the daily routine of bowel movements, gargling, washing my face, eating breakfast, etc., and it was already 8:15. That's terrible! I hurriedly grabbed a newspaper and hurriedly left the gate, squeezing into the third-class carriage of a tram. Because I was walking too fast, I was constantly panting.

At this time, it is the so-called Officehour in Shanghai. The time for buses to collect money is called "busy time". This time is really busy. Look, the third-class carriages, the trailers, and even the first-class trams and buses are full of crowds heading towards the Bund.

The car stopped for a while at a turning point, and my old friend Zhang also squeezed up from the crowd.

"Mr. Zhang! How are you?" I sent my voice over from the shoulder of a person.

"Ah! Are you here too? ... What's good or bad? Still living the 'Four Heads' life." Zhang replied and squeezed in front of me.

"What! 'Four Heads' life! What..."

"Aren't you also a junior office worker in a company?" He said: "How can you not understand this 'Four Heads' life? Haha! Let me tell you!" So he started talking.

"Doesn't your company open at nine o'clock? Don't you have to rush there at 8:15? Aren't you squeezing in here because you're afraid of being late? Of course, you have to get to the office before nine o'clock no matter what. But if you are a manager, a supervisor, or some senior employee, then you can go slowly. It doesn't matter if you go at eleven o'clock. So, junior office workers have to arrive 'ahead' of others. This is the first 'head'."

"Um..."

"Even if you are exhausted, you can't leave until the bell rings at five o'clock in the afternoon. Sometimes, you even have to wait until 5:30 or 6:00 to have hope of getting out of the gate. However, managers, supervisors, and other senior employees disappear at three o'clock. This is called leaving 'behind' others. This is the second 'head'."

"On the day of paying salaries, the salary envelopes of senior employees are thick with colorful piles of banknotes, while ours are only a few thin sheets, at most, only other peoples' 'change,' this is the third 'head'. If things are done slightly less than perfect, the iron faces of senior employees will sink, and they will scold you a few times! Ouch! This is the fourth 'head'."

"Coming ahead, leaving behind, taking the change, eating the scolding, isn't this the 'Four Heads' life? Haha! Brother! You and I are living the same 'Four Heads' life!" Zhang shouted loudly.

The car happened to reach its destination, so I said goodbye to Zhang and squeezed out of the car. I rushed to the office. Ah! I'm the first one.

"Ah! 'Four Heads' life!" I tasted it wistfully like this.
